</tr><tr><td style="padding:0.3em 0.4em 0.3em;font-weight:bold;border-top: 1px solid #aaa; border-bottom: 1px solid #aaa;">
<ul><li><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Emblem-money.svg"><img alt="Emblem-money.svg" class="noviewer" data-file-height="48" data-file-width="48" decoding="async" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Emblem-money.svg/16px-Emblem-money.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Emblem-money.svg/24px-Emblem-money.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Emblem-money.svg/32px-Emblem-money.svg.png 2x" width="16"/></a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Portal:Business_and_economics" title="Portal:Business and economics">Business and economics portal</a></li></ul></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Business_administration" title="Template:Business administration"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Business_administration" title="Template talk:Business administration"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Business_administration&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>A <b>business entity</b> is an entity that is formed and administered as per <a href="/wiki/Corporate_law" title="Corporate law">corporate law</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Exception_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-Exception-1">[Note 1]</a></sup> in order to engage in <a href="/wiki/Business" title="Business">business</a> activities, charitable work, or other activities allowable. Most often, business entities are formed to sell a product or a service.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> There are many types of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Business_entities" title="Business entities">business entities</a> defined in the legal systems of various countries. These include <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperatives</a>, <a href="/wiki/Partnership" title="Partnership">partnerships</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_trader" title="Sole trader">sole traders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability companies</a> and other specifically permitted and labelled types of entities. The specific rules vary by country and by state or province. Some of these types are listed below, by country.
</p><p>For guidance, approximate equivalents in the company law of English-speaking countries are given in most cases, for example:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">private company limited by shares</a> or Ltd. (UK, Ireland and the Commonwealth)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">public limited company</a> (UK, Ireland and the Commonwealth)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chartered_company" title="Chartered company">chartered company</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Statutory_corporation" title="Statutory corporation">statutory corporation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/State-owned_enterprise" title="State-owned enterprise">state-owned enterprise</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Holding_company" title="Holding company">holding company</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subsidiary" title="Subsidiary">subsidiary company</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charitable_incorporated_organisation" title="Charitable incorporated organisation">charitable incorporated organisation</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Reciprocal_inter-insurance_exchange" title="Reciprocal inter-insurance exchange">reciprocal inter-insurance exchange</a></li></ul>
<p>However, the regulations governing particular types of entities, even those described as roughly equivalent, differ from jurisdiction to jurisdiction. When creating or restructuring a business, the legal responsibilities will depend on the type of business entity chosen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[1]</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Albania">Albania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Albania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span class="anchor" id="Business_registration_in_Albania"></span> Foreign and domestic investors have a range of opportunities to organize their business in <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>. They can either establish and register a business organization or establish and register a branch or representative office.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[2]</a></sup> The registration of foreign entities, since 1 September 2007, had been carried out at the National Registration Center, which aimed to implement the "one stop shop" system. Law No. 131/2015 dated 26 November 2015<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[3]</a></sup> made possible the creation of the <a href="/wiki/National_Business_Center_(Albania)" title="National Business Center (Albania)">National Business Center (QKB)</a>, whose purpose was to simplify the procedures of doing business in the country by enabling registration and licensing procedures in a single institution. As a result, the National Registration Center and the National Licensing Center were abolished.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[4]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Sh.p.k. (Shoqëri me përgjegjësi të kufizuar): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK); a business entity established by one or several <a href="/wiki/Natural_person" title="Natural person">natural</a> or <a href="/wiki/Legal_person" title="Legal person">legal</a> persons;</li>
<li>Sh.A. (Shoqëri Aksionere): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">PLC</a> (UK); a company whose capital is divided into shares signed by its founders;</li>
<li>Shoqëri komandite: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a>; the liability of at least one partner is limited to the value of their contribution;</li>
<li>Shoqëri kolektive: ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a>; the liability of the company's partners before its creditors is unlimited;</li>
<li>Degë: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Subsidiary" title="Subsidiary">subsidiary</a>; entities created by a parent company that carry the same legal presence as the company;</li>
<li>Zyrë e përfaqësimit: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Representative_office" title="Representative office">representative office</a>; business offices where a company's activities can operate from that are not intended to generate revenue.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Argentina">Argentina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Argentina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>S.A.S (corporation)| S.A.S (Sociedades de Acciones Simplificadas):</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>S.R.L. (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[5]</a></sup> (USA)</li>
<li>S.C.S. (Sociedad en Comandita Simple): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>S.C.p.A. (Sociedad en Comandita por Acciones): <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a> with shares</li>
<li>Soc.Col. (Sociedad Colectiva): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> (USA)</li>
<li>S.C.e I. (Sociedad de Capital e Industria)</li>
<li>S.E. (Sociedad del Estado): ≈ <a href="/wiki/State-owned_enterprise" title="State-owned enterprise">state-owned enterprise</a></li>
<li>S.G.R. (Sociedad de Garantía Reciproca)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[6]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[7]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>LLP (<a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Limited liability partnership</a>): partnerships are governed on a state-by-state basis in Australia. In Queensland, a limited liability partnership is composed of at least one general partner and one limited partner. It is thus similar to what is called a limited partnership in many countries.</li>
<li>ILP (Incorporated limited partnership): used for venture capital investments comes in four types: Venture Capital Limited Partnership (VCLP), Early-stage Venture Capital Limited Partnership (ESCVLP), Australian Venture Capital Fund of Funds (AFOF), Venture Capital Management Partnership (VCMP).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[8]</a></sup>
<ul><li><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Corporations_Act_2001" title="Corporations Act 2001">Corporations Act 2001</a></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Inc. (Incorporated): restricted to non-profit associations</li>
<li>Ltd. (Limited): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). The suffix Ltd. may also be used by a private company limited by guarantee, such as a charity or university (these may obtain dispensation from the Registrar of Companies to operate without the suffix).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/No_liability" title="No liability">NL</a> (No liability): A type of mining, speculative, or research company with no right to call up the unpaid issue price of shares.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pty._Ltd." title="Pty. Ltd.">Pty. Ltd.</a> (Proprietary Limited Company): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK) ATF Trust. In Australia companies can act as a trustee for a trust.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">Pty.</a> (Unlimited Proprietary) company with a share capital: A company, similar to its limited company (Ltd., or Pty. Ltd.) counterpart, but where the liability of the members or shareholders is not limited.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Austria">Austria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Austria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Gen (Genossenschaft; types: Erwerbs- und Wirtschaftsgenossenschaft): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li>
<li>Privatstiftung: ≈ private foundation</li>
<li>Verein: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">nonprofit association</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Types_of_business_entity#European_Economic_Area_(including_the_European_Union)" title="Types of business entity">European business entities</a></li>
<li>e.U. (eingetragenes Einzelunternehmen): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_trader" title="Sole trader">sole trader</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (US)</li>
<li>Kapitalgesellschaften: ≈ companies
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Aktiengesellschaft): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum capital €70,000.</li>
<li>GmbH (<a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung</a>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Minimum capital €35,000.</li></ul></li>
<li>Personengesellschaften: ≈ partnerships
<ul><li><i>unincorporated (i.e. unregistered and without legal personality)</i>:
<ul><li>stG (stille Gesellschaft): ≈ partnership by estoppel (i.e., no partnership agreement)</li>
<li>GesbR (Gesellschaft des bürgerlichen Rechts): ≈ partnership by contract (i.e., formed by partnership agreement); statutes and regulations concerning Austrian companies, especially with regards to the companies register (<i>Firmenbuch</i>), do not apply.</li></ul></li>
<li><i>incorporated (i.e. registered and with legal personality)</i>:
<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Offene_Gesellschaft&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Offene Gesellschaft (page does not exist)">OG</a> (offene Gesellschaft): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">KG</a> (Kommanditgesellschaft): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a>
<ul><li>GmbH &amp; Co. KG: <a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">KG</a> in which a <a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">GmbH</a> is the general partner.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>Obsolete:
<ul><li>Erwerbsgesellschaft: small-sized partnerships (not qualifying as <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Offene_Gesellschaft&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Offene Gesellschaft (page does not exist)">OG</a> or <a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">KG</a>, respectively. Converted into OGs or KGs as of 1. 1. 2007)
<ul><li>OEG (Offene Erwerbsgesellschaft): small general partnership</li>
<li>KEG (Kommanditerwerbsgesellschaft): small limited partnership</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><small>See also <a class="external text" href="https://www.usp.gv.at/Portal.Node/usp/public/content/gruendung/gruendungsfahrplan_gesellschaften/gesellschaftsformen/Seite.470202.html" rel="nofollow">help.gv.at</a> (Austrian government site, in German)</small>
</p>

<p>Following changes to the Code of Companies and Associations, the term "Private limited liability company" (BVBA/SPRL) automatically became "Private limited company" (BV/SRL),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FR_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-FR-10">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NL_11-0"><a href="#cite_note-NL-11">[10]</a></sup> as a part of harmonising legal entity types within the European Union.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bosnia_and_Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Bosnia and Herzegovina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>d.d. (dioničko društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Germany)</li>
<li>a.d. (akcionarsko društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Germany)</li>
<li>d.n.o. (društvo s neograničenom solidarnom odgovornošću): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>d.o.o. (društvo s ograničenom odgovornošću): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">GmbH</a> (Germany)</li>
<li>k.d. (komanditno društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>s.p. (samostalni preduzetnik): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a> (UK)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil">Brazil</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Brazil">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Sociedade limitada (Ltda.): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedade anônima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>Sociedade simples: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PLLC" title="PLLC">PLLC</a></li>
<li>Sociedade em comandita simples: ≈ ordinary limited partnership</li>
<li>Sociedade em nome coletivo: ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>Sociedade em conta de participação: ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>Sociedade em comum: ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>Cooperativa ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li>
<li>Empresa individual (firma individual): ≈ individual proprietorship / sole proprietorship</li>
<li>Empresa Individual de Responsabilidade Limitada (EIRELI): Same as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a>, but without partners.</li>
<li>Micro empreendedor individual: ≈ individual enterprise</li>
<li>Empresa pública: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government-owned_corporation" title="Government-owned corporation">Government-owned corporation</a></li>
<li>Sociedade de economia mista: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government-owned_corporation" title="Government-owned corporation">Government-owned corporation</a></li>
<li>Associação em sentido estrito (sem finalidade lucrativa): ≈ nonprofit association</li>
<li>Organização não governamental: ≈ nonprofit association</li>
<li>Organização da sociedade civil de interesse público: ≈ nonprofit association</li>
<li>Organização social: ≈ nonprofit association</li>
<li>Serviços sociais autônomos: ≈ nonprofit association</li>
<li>Fundação privada: ≈ private foundation</li>
<li>Fundação pública: ≈ public foundation</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brunei">Brunei</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Brunei">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There are three main types of business entity in Brunei, namely <b>sole proprietorship</b>, <b>partnership</b> and <b>company</b>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup>
</p><p>A private company contains the term "Sendirian Berhad" or "Sdn. Bhd." as part of its name; for a public company "Berhad" or "Bhd." is used.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[12]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Bulgaria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>AD / <i>АД</i> (aktsionerno drujestvo / <i>акционерно дружество</i>): <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joint_stock_company" title="Joint stock company">joint stock company</a> ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>ADSITs / <i>АДСИЦ</i> (aktsionerno druzhestvo sus spetsialna investitsionna tsel / <i>акционерно дружество със специална инвестиционна цел</i>): <a href="/wiki/Real_estate_investment_trust" title="Real estate investment trust">real estate investment trust</a></li>
<li>EAD / <i>ЕАД</i> (ednolichno aktsionerno druzhestvo / <i>еднолично акционерно дружество</i>): type <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a></li>
<li>EOOD / <i>ЕООД</i> (ednolichno druzhestvo s ogranichena otgovornost / <i>еднолично дружество с ограничена отговорност</i>): type of OOD with a single member</li>
<li>ET / <i>ЕТ</i> (ednolichen turgovetz / <i>едноличен търговец</i>): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>OOD / <i>ООД</i> (drujestvo s ogranichena otgovornost / <i>дружество с ограничена отговорност</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>KD / <i>КД</i> (komanditno druzhestvo / <i>командитно дружество</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>KDA / <i>КДА</i> (komanditno druzhestvo s aktzii / <i>командитно дружество с акции</i>): limited partnership with shares</li>
<li>SD / <i>СД</i> (subiratelno druzhestvo / <i>събирателно дружество</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a>, but having <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legal_personality" title="Legal personality">legal personality</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cambodian">Cambodian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Cambodian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SP (Sole Proprietorship)</li>
<li>GP (General Partnership)</li>
<li>LP (Limited Partnership)</li>
<li>SM Pte Ltd. (Single Member Private Limited Company):</li>
<li>Pte Ltd. (Private Limited Company): ≈ [private limited company (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a>)] (UK)</li>
<li>Plc Ltd. (Public Limited Company): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>PEEC (Public Establishment with Economic characteristics)</li>
<li>State Company: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a></li>
<li>State Joint Venture Company: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a></li>
<li>Import Export Co., Ltd</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Canada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In Canada entities can be incorporated under either federal or provincial (or territorial) law.
</p><p>The word or expression "Limited", <i>Limitée</i>, "Incorporated", <i>Incorporée</i>, "Corporation" or <i>Société par actions de régime fédéral</i> or the corresponding abbreviation "Ltd.", <i>Ltée</i>, "Inc.", "Corp." or <i>S.A.R.F.</i> forms part of the name of every entity incorporated under the <a href="/wiki/Canada_Business_Corporations_Act" title="Canada Business Corporations Act">Canada Business Corporations Act</a> (R.S., 1985, c. C-44). ≈ Ltd. or Plc (UK)
</p><p>As an exception, entities registered prior to 1985 may continue to be designated <i>Société commerciale canadienne</i> or by the abbreviation <i>S.C.C.</i>
</p><p>Under the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Canada_Cooperatives_Act&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Canada Cooperatives Act (page does not exist)">Canada Cooperatives Act</a> (1998, c. 1), a co-operative must have the word "cooperative", "co-operative", "coop", "co-op", <i>coopérative</i>, "united" or "pool", or another grammatical form of any of those words, as part of its name.
</p><p>Unlike in many other Western countries, Canadian businesses generally only have one form of incorporation available. <a href="/wiki/Unlimited_liability_corporation" title="Unlimited liability corporation">Unlimited liability corporations</a> can be formed in Alberta "AULC", British Columbia "BCULC"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[13]</a></sup> and Nova Scotia "NSULC". The aforementioned unlimited liability corporations are generally not used as operating business structures, but are instead used to create favorable tax positions for either Americans investing in Canada or vice versa.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[14]</a></sup> For U.S. tax purposes the ULC is classified as a disregarded entity.
</p><p>Rather, Canadian businesses are generally formed under one of the following structures:
</p>
<ul><li>SP (Sole Proprietorship): No formal business structure is established</li>
<li>GP (General Partnership): Either a formal structure with a partnership agreement, or an informal structure, in which case the Partnerships Act for the province will apply</li>
<li>LP (Limited Partnership): An investment structure, limiting both the liability and the participation of the investor. An investor who takes an active role will be deemed a general partner, and become exposed to unlimited liability.</li>
<li>Corporation</li>
<li>Joint Venture: A business activity shared by two or more business entities. The joint venture's activities must be finite in terms of either time or scope.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Chile">Chile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Chile">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SpA (Sociedad por acciones): Disregarded entity with shares (sole shareholder)</li>
<li>SRL (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitdada) – LLC (Partnership) US purposes</li>
<li>EIRL (Empresa Individual de Responsabilidad Limitada): individual enterprise with limited liability</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>S.G.R. (Sociedad de Garantia Reciproca)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li>LTDA. (Sociedad de responsabilidad limitada): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>有限公司 (<i lang="zh-Latn-pinyin" title="Chinese language text">Yǒuxiàn Gōngsī</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). See also <a href="/wiki/Partnership_(China)" title="Partnership (China)">Partnership (China)</a>.</li>
<li>股份有限公司 (<i lang="zh-Latn-pinyin" title="Chinese language text">Gǔfèn Yǒuxiàn Gōngsī</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Joint-stock_company" title="Joint-stock company">joint-stock company</a>, <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a>.</li>
<li>无限责任公司 (<i lang="zh-Latn-pinyin" title="Chinese language text">Wúxiàn Zérèn Gōngsī</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unlimited_liability_company" title="Unlimited liability company">unlimited liability company</a>.</li>
<li>有限责任股份公司 (<i lang="zh-Latn-pinyin" title="Chinese language text">Yǒuxiàn Zérèn Gǔfèn Gōngsī</i>): ≈ share-holding limited liability company.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Colombia">Colombia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Colombia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a></b> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corporation</a> (US)</li>
<li><b>S.A.S.</b> (Sociedades por Acciones Simplificada): Similar to the French S.A.S (<i>societé par actions simplifiée</i>)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Ltda.</b> (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US)</li>
<li><b>S.C.</b> (Sociedad Colectiva): <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a></li>
<li><b>S. en C.</b> (Comandita Simple): <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">Limited partnership</a></li>
<li><b>S.C.A.</b> (Comandita por Acciones): Publicly traded partnership</li>
<li><b>E.U.</b> (Empresa Unipersonal): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Costa_Rica">Costa Rica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Costa Rica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>S.A.</b> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corporation</a> (US)</li>
<li><b>S.R.L.</b> or <b>Ltda.</b> (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US) <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[17]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Croatia">Croatia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Croatia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Types of legal person business entities:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[18]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><b>d.d.</b> (dioničko društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)  ≈ <a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Germany)</li>
<li><b>d.o.o.</b> (društvo s ograničenom odgovornošću) is company with limited liability: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK) or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LLC" title="LLC">LLC</a> (US); minimum capital: <a href="/wiki/Croatian_kuna" title="Croatian kuna">HRK</a> 20,000<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>j.d.o.o.</b> (jednostavno društvo s ograničenom odgovornošću): simple Ltd.; minimum capital: HRK 10 (same liabilities as an Ltd., but has to set aside 25% of annual profit to collect enough equity capital to become a d.o.o.)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>j.t.d.</b> (javno trgovačko društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li><b>k.d.</b> (komanditno društvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li><b>GIU</b> (gospodarsko interesno udruženje): economic interest grouping</li>
<li><b>zadruga</b>: <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[21]</a></sup></li></ul>
<p>Types of natural person business entities:
</p>
<ul><li><b>obrt</b>: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a>; several types: <i>slobodni obrt</i> (free proprietorship), <i>vezani obrt</i> (tied proprietorship), and <i>povlašteni obrt</i> (privileged proprietorship) registered according to profession where tied and privileged types are reserved only for master craftsmen): <i>paušalni obrt</i> (flat-rate proprietorship), <i>obrt-dohodaš</i> (income tax proprietorship), <i>obrt-dobitaš</i> (profits tax proprietorship); these are registered according to the type of taxation; first two are obligated to pay income tax and the last one is obligated to pay profits tax), <i>sezonski obrt</i> (seasonal proprietorship) that runs for a limited number of months during a year.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>ortakluk</b>: partnership of two or more sole proprietors</li>
<li><b>slobodna djelatnost</b>: free profession; <a href="/wiki/Self-employment" title="Self-employment">self-employment</a> but only for certain types of professions: e.g. artists, journalists, lawyers, etc.; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Freelancing" title="Freelancing">freelancing</a> (similar to sole proprietors in their obligations)</li>
<li><b>domaća radinost</b> and <b>sporedno zanimanje</b>: home business and side profession; limited forms of self-employment aimed at registering supplementary income from, say, small repairs or hobbies with yearly income limited to 10 average gross salaries (approx. EUR 11,700 in January 2020)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>OPG</b> (obiteljsko poljoprivredno gospodarstvo): family run agricultural business<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[24]</a></sup></li></ul>
<p>Non-profit:
</p>
<ul><li><b>udruga</b> ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">voluntary association</a>; any form of free and voluntary association of natural or legal persons to accomplish a purpose without intent to acquire profit.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[25]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Czech Republic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Akciov%C3%A1_spole%C4%8Dnost" title="Akciová společnost">a.s.</a>, akc. spol. (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Akciov%C3%A1_spole%C4%8Dnost" title="Akciová společnost">Akciová společnost</a>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum share capital <a href="/wiki/Czech_koruna" title="Czech koruna">CZK</a> 2 000 000. Must have a <a href="/wiki/Supervisory_board" title="Supervisory board">supervisory board</a> in addition to the management board.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Spole%C4%8Dnost_s_ru%C4%8Den%C3%ADm_omezen%C3%BDm" title="Společnost s ručením omezeným">s.r.o.</a>, spol. s r.o. (<a href="/wiki/Spole%C4%8Dnost_s_ru%C4%8Den%C3%ADm_omezen%C3%BDm" title="Společnost s ručením omezeným">Společnost s ručením omezeným</a>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK) Minimum share capital <a href="/wiki/Czech_koruna" title="Czech koruna">CZK</a> 1<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li>v.o.s. (veřejná obchodní společnost): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>k.s. (komanditní společnost): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>o.p.s. (<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Obecn%C4%9B_prosp%C4%9B%C5%A1n%C3%A1_spole%C4%8Dnost&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Obecně prospěšná společnost (page does not exist)">obecně prospěšná společnost</a>): ≈ One of the legal forms for non-governmental non-profit organizations</li>
<li>živnost: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>s.p. (státní podnik): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_enterprise" title="State enterprise">state enterprise</a></li>
<li>příspěvková organizace: ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Subsidized_organization&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Subsidized organization (page does not exist)">subsidized organization</a></li>
<li>z.s. (zapsaný spolek) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">Voluntary association</a>. Formerly o.s. (Občanské sdružení.)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Denmark">Denmark</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Denmark">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">"K/S" redirects here. For the pairing, see <a href="/wiki/Kirk/Spock" title="Kirk/Spock">Kirk/Spock</a>.</div>
<ul><li>Enkeltmandsvirksomhed: <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>Forening: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">association</a></li>
<li>I/S (Interessentskab): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a>.</li>
<li>IVS (Iværksætterselskab): <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">private limited company</a> startup with limited equity capital. Must use 25% of profit to collect enough equity capital to become an ApS.</li>
<li>ApS (Anpartsselskab): <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">private limited company</a>.</li>
<li>A/S (Aktieselskab): <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">public limited company</a>.</li>
<li>K/S (Kommanditselskab): <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>P/S (Partnerselskab <i>or</i> Kommanditaktieselskab): <a href="/wiki/Partnership_limited_by_shares" title="Partnership limited by shares">partnership limited by shares</a></li>
<li>A.M.B.A. (Andelsselskab med begrænset ansvar): limited liability <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Co-operative" title="Co-operative">co-operative</a>.</li>
<li>F.M.B.A. (Forening med begrænset ansvar): limited liability <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">voluntary association</a>.</li>
<li>S.M.B.A. (Selskab med begrænset ansvar): <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a>.</li>
<li>Partsrederi: A form of combined and continued ownership of a merchant vessel.</li>
<li>Erhvervsdrivende fond: <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Commercial_foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Commercial foundation (page does not exist)">commercial foundation</a></li>
<li>G/S (Gensidigt selskab): <a href="/wiki/Mutual_organization" title="Mutual organization">mutual organization</a></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Egypt">Egypt</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Egypt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SAE (Sharikat al-Mossahamah) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Pound" title="Egyptian Pound">EGP</a> 250,000.</li>
<li>LLC (Limited Liability Company) ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). No Minimum capital .</li>
<li>Sharikat Tadamun ≈ شركة تضامن <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>Sharikat Tawssiyah Bassita ≈ شركات توصية بسيطة <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>Sharikat Tawssiyah Belashom ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">LLP</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Estonia">Estonia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Estonia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>FIE (Füüsilisest isikust ettevõtja): ≈ sole trader (UK), sole proprietorship (US)</li>
<li>Partnerships:
<ul><li>UÜ (Usaldusühing): ≈ limited partnership</li>
<li>TÜ (Täisühing): ≈ general partnership</li></ul></li>
<li>Companies:
<ul><li>OÜ (Osaühing): ≈ (Ltd.) private limited company (UK), (LLC) limited liability company (US)</li>
<li>AS (Aktsiaselts): ≈ (PLC) public limited company (UK), corporation (US)</li></ul></li>
<li>Tulundusühistu: ≈ commercial association</li>
<li>MTÜ (Mittetulundusühing) ≈ nonprofit organization</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Ethiopia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>PLC (Private limited company Amharic ሃላፊነቱ የተወሰነ የግል ማህበር)</li>
<li>SC (Share company Amharic አክሲዩን ማህበር)</li>
<li>CS (cooperative societies Amharic ህብረት ስራ ማህበራት)</li>
<li>PE or PC (public enterprises or public corporations Amharic የመንግስት ልማት ድርጅቶች or ኮርፖሬሽን)</li></ul>
<h2><span id="European_Economic_Area_.28including_the_European_Union.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="European_Economic_Area_(including_the_European_Union)">European Economic Area (including the European Union)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: European Economic Area (including the European Union)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Partnerships:
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/European_economic_interest_grouping" title="European economic interest grouping">European economic interest grouping</a> (EEIG): an EU legal entity designed to enable cross-border cooperation between companies. It has <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unlimited_liability" title="Unlimited liability">unlimited liability</a> and is not liable for <a href="/wiki/Corporate_tax" title="Corporate tax">corporate tax</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Companies:
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Societas_cooperativa_Europaea" title="Societas cooperativa Europaea">Societas cooperativa Europaea</a> (SCE): a European <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a> (Latin for "European Cooperative Society").</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Societas_Europaea" title="Societas Europaea">Societas Europaea</a> (SE): a European (Public) Limited Company (Latin for "European Company").</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Societas_privata_Europaea" title="Societas privata Europaea">Societas privata Europaea</a> (SPE): a European private limited company, corresponding to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GmbH" title="GmbH">GmbH</a>, etc. (Latin for "European Private Company"). This form of company is currently being proposed by the <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<p>An SE or SCE may be created by registration in any of the EU/EEA member states and may relocate its registered office to any other member state with minimal formalities.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Finland">Finland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Finland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dt>General economic entities</dt></dl>
<ul><li>Ay (avoin yhtiö, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">öppet bolag</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> (use optional)</li>
<li>Ky (kommandiittiyhtiö, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">kommanditbolag</i>, <i>Kb</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>Oy (<a href="/wiki/Osakeyhti%C3%B6" title="Osakeyhtiö">osakeyhtiö</a>, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">aktiebolag</i>, <i>Ab</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). No minimum <a href="/wiki/Share_capital" title="Share capital">share capital</a> as of 01.07.2019.</li>
<li>Oyj (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Julkinen_osakeyhti%C3%B6" title="Julkinen osakeyhtiö">julkinen osakeyhtiö</a>, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">publikt aktiebolag</i>, <i>Abp</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>osk (osuuskunta, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">andelslag</i>, <i>Anl.</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li>
<li>T:mi (toiminimi), Yksityinen elinkeinonharjoittaja (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">firma</i>/<i>F:ma</i>, <i>enskild näringsidkare</i>): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (use optional)</li></ul>
<p>The abbreviations are usually in Finnish, but <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a> names may also be used either as is or in combination with Finnish, e.g. <i>Oy Yritys Ab</i>.
</p>
<dl><dt>Non-profit entities</dt></dl>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rekister%C3%B6ity_yhdistys" title="Rekisteröity yhdistys">rekisteröity yhdistys</a>, abbr. ry (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">förening</i>, abbr. rf): registered <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">association</a>, capable of acting as a legal person</li>
<li>rekisteröity puolue, abbr. rp <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">registrerat parti</i>): registered political party</li>
<li>säätiö, abbr. rs (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">stiftelse</i>): foundation</li>
<li>uskonnollinen yhdyskunta (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">religionssamfund</i>), religious community<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>voluntary associations chartered by statute law (e.g. Finnish <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red_Cross" title="Red Cross">Red Cross</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[30]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/National_Defence_Training_Association_of_Finland" title="National Defence Training Association of Finland">National Defence Training Association of Finland</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Finnish_Bar_Association&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Finnish Bar Association (page does not exist)">Finnish Bar Association</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[31]</a></sup>)</li></ul>
<dl><dt>For-profit entities of public law</dt></dl>
<ul><li>valtion liikelaitos (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">statens affärsverk</i>): commercial government agency, expected to fund themselves, but debts directly backed by state funds—distinguished from regular companies where the government owns stock. (See: <a href="/wiki/List_of_Finnish_government_enterprises" title="List of Finnish government enterprises">List of Finnish government enterprises</a>)</li>
<li>kunnallinen liikelaitos (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">kommunal affärsverk</i>): municipal enterprise, similar as previous but run by a <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Finland" title="Municipalities of Finland">municipality</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Siida" title="Siida">paliskunta</a>: a reindeer herding corporation, governed like a stock company except that the "stocks" are reindeer<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[32]</a></sup></li></ul>
<dl><dt>Economic entities for special purpose</dt></dl>
<ul><li>asunto-osakeyhtiö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">bostadsaktiebolag</i>), a limited liability company for the ownership, construction and maintenance of an apartment building<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li>julkinen keskinäinen vakuutusyhtiö, abbreviated jy (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">publikt ömsesidigt försäkringsbolag</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vakuutusyhtiölaki_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vakuutusyhtiölaki-35">[34]</a></sup> public mutual insurance company</li>
<li>keskinäinen kiinteistöosakeyhtiö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">ömsesidiga fastighetsaktiebolag</i>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[35]</a></sup> a limited liability company for the ownership, maintenance and construction of real property.</li>
<li>keskinäinen vakuutusyhtiö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">ömsesidigt försäkringsbolag</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vakuutusyhtiölaki_35-1"><a href="#cite_note-Vakuutusyhtiölaki-35">[34]</a></sup> mutual insurance company</li>
<li>laivaisännistöyhtiö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">partrederi</i>), a type of general partnership for the owning of a <a href="/wiki/Cargo_ship" title="Cargo ship">merchantman</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li>säästöpankki (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">sparbank</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[37]</a></sup> a type of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Loans_and_savings_association&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Loans and savings association (page does not exist)">loans and savings association</a></li></ul>
<dl><dt>Real estate law corporations</dt></dl>
<p>In the corporations of real estate law, the ownership or membership may be vested either in the real property or in a legal or natural person, depending on the corporation type. In many cases, the membership or ownership of such corporation is obligatory for a person or property that fulfils the legal requirements for membership or wishes to engage in certain activities.
</p>
<ul><li>keskivedenkorkeuden muuttamista varten perustettu yhteisö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">Sammanslutning som bildas för höjning av medelvattenståndet</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[38]</a></sup> a corporation of water law for the permanent change of the median water level</li>
<li>ojitusyhteisö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">dikningssammanslutning</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vesilaki_587/2011_40-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vesilaki_587/2011-40">[39]</a></sup> a corporation of water law for the construction and maintenance of ditches</li>
<li>säännöstely-yhteisö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">regleringssammanslutning</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vesilaki_587/2011_40-1"><a href="#cite_note-Vesilaki_587/2011-40">[39]</a></sup> a corporation of water law for the regulation of water level in a body of water</li>
<li>tiekunta (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">väglag</i>), a type of limited-liability corporation for the maintenance of private road<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li>uittoyhteisö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">flottningssammanslutning</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[41]</a></sup> a corporation of water law for timber-floating</li>
<li>vesioikeudellinen yhteisö (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">vattenrättslig sammanslutning</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[42]</a></sup> a corporation of water law for a project that involves economic use of bodies of water</li>
<li>yhteisalue (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">samfälliga område</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44">[43]</a></sup> a corporation for the maintenance of a real property jointly used by several other properties or persons</li>
<li>yhteismetsä (<a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">samfälld skog</i>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45">[44]</a></sup> a jointly owned forest</li>
<li>osakaskunta (historically "jakokunta"), a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Partition_unit" title="Partition unit">partition unit</a>, i.e. a corporation for maintenance of the commons.</li></ul>
<p>In addition to native types, European Union types are implemented:
</p>
<ul><li>SE (Eurooppayhtiö), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_Company_Statute" title="European Company Statute">European Company</a></li>
<li>SCE (Eurooppaosuuskunta), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_Cooperative_Society" title="European Cooperative Society">European Cooperative Society</a></li>
<li>EEIG (Eurooppalainen taloudellinen etuyhtymä, <a href="/wiki/Swedish_language" title="Swedish language">Swedish</a>: <i lang="sv">europeisk ekonomisk intressegruppering</i>), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_Economic_Interest_Grouping" title="European Economic Interest Grouping">European Economic Interest Grouping</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="France">France</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: France">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Micro-entreprise: special framework for <a href="/wiki/Small_business#Size_definitions" title="Small business">minute businesses</a>, a recent addition to French business law -with both revenue and pre-tax net income caps, of which Auto-entrepreneur (below) is a special case</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freelancer" title="Freelancer">Freelancers</a>, individual <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Independent_contractor" title="Independent contractor">independent contractors</a>:
<ul><li>Auto-entrepreneur: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-employed" title="Self-employed">self-employed</a> (UK), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Independent_contractor" title="Independent contractor">independent contractor</a> (US), a recent addition to French business law -with both a revenue cap and a specific set of derogatory <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">income tax</a> rates</li>
<li>Profession libérale: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> such as a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Medical_practice" title="Medical practice">medical practice</a>, an enduring entity stemming from the protected status designed for "<a href="/wiki/Profession" title="Profession">liberal professions</a>" with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_Trader_Insolvency" title="Sole Trader Insolvency">unlimited personal liability</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9s_d%27exercice_lib%C3%A9ral&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sociétés d'exercice libéral (page does not exist)">Sociétés d'exercice libéral</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_d%27exercice_lib%C3%A9ral" title="fr:Société d'exercice libéral">fr</a>]</sup>: the incorporated equivalent of the latter, sole shareholder <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability" title="Limited liability">limited liability</a> being key</li>
<li>EI (Entreprise individuelle/entreprise en nom personnel):</li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Investment_fund" title="Investment fund">Investment funds</a>/companies:
<ul><li>FCP (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fond_commun_de_placement" title="Fond commun de placement">Fond commun de placement</a>): unincorporated investment fund</li>
<li>Société d'investissement à capital fixe: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Investment_trust" title="Investment trust">investment trust</a> (UK); <a href="/wiki/Closed-end_fund" title="Closed-end fund">closed-end fund</a> (CEF), closed-end company (US); listed investment company (LIC) (Au)</li>
<li>SICAV (Société d'investissement à capital variable): ≈ investment company with variable capital (ICVC), <a href="/wiki/Open-ended_investment_company" title="Open-ended investment company">open-ended investment company</a> (OEIC) (UK); <a href="/wiki/Mutual_fund" title="Mutual fund">mutual fund</a>, open-end company (US)</li></ul></li>
<li>GIE (Groupement d'intérêt économique): economic interest grouping</li>
<li>Association: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">nonprofit association</a>
<ul><li>Association non-déclarée: ≈ unincorporated association (UK)</li>
<li>Association déclarée: ≈ incorporated association (Au)</li></ul></li>
<li>Partnerships (<i>société de personnes</i>):
<ul><li>SEP (Société en participation): ≈ equity partnership</li>
<li>SNC (Société en nom collectif): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> (GP)</li>
<li>SCS (Société en commandite simple): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a> (LP)</li>
<li>SCA (Société en commandite par actions): ≈ publicly traded partnership (PTP) (US)</li>
<li>SCI (Société Civile Immobilière): ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=French_property_company_(SCI)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="French property company (SCI) (page does not exist)">French property company (SCI)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Companies (<i>société de capitaux</i>):
<ul><li>share companies (both partnership and company)
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_%C3%A0_responsabilit%C3%A9_limit%C3%A9e" title="Société à responsabilité limitée">SARL</a>, SàRL (Société à responsabilité limitée): ≈ private limited company (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a>) (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a> (US)
<ul><li>EURL (Entreprise unipersonnelle à responsabilité limitée): ≈ single shareholder limited company (SME Pvt) (UK)</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>stock companies (<i>société par actions</i>)
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">SA</a> (Société anonyme): ≈ public limited company (<a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a>) (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a> (US/Can)
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_coop%C3%A9rative" title="Société coopérative">SCOP</a> (Société coopérative de production): ≈ cooperative corporation (Can)</li>
<li>SEM (Société d'économie mixte): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government-owned_corporation" title="Government-owned corporation">government-owned corporation</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_par_actions_simplifi%C3%A9e" title="Société par actions simplifiée">SAS</a> (Société par actions simplifiée): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a> (US, <a href="/wiki/Delaware_General_Corporation_Law" title="Delaware General Corporation Law">especially in Delaware</a>), unlisted public company (Au), close corporation (CC) (S. Africa), private corporation (Can); often used for <a href="/wiki/Subsidiary" title="Subsidiary">subsidiaries</a>; minimum of one director and two members/shareholders; no limit on share capital; liability can be restricted to director; no "one share – one vote" principle
<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_par_actions_simplifi%C3%A9e_unipersonnelle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Société par actions simplifiée unipersonnelle (page does not exist)">SASU</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_par_actions_simplifi%C3%A9e_unipersonnelle" title="fr:Société par actions simplifiée unipersonnelle">fr</a>]</span> (U- unipersonnelle): limited liability, sole shareholder <a href="/wiki/Limited_company" title="Limited company">Ltd. company</a> (UK) or single member close corporation</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Germany">Germany</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Germany">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>individuals
<ul><li><i>Einzelunternehmen</i>: individual entrepreneur ≈ sole trader (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a>; only professional services, agriculture and forestry as well as small commercial businesses</li>
<li><i>Eingetragener Kaufmann</i> (male/both genders)/<i>eingetragene Kauffrau</i> (female) (e.K./e.Kfm./e.Kfr.): registered merchant ≈ sole trader (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (US); individual entrepreneur with commercial business (<i>Handelsgewerbe</i>)</li></ul></li>
<li>partnerships (<i>Personengesellschaften</i> )
<ul><li><i>Gesellschaft bürgerlichen Rechts</i> (<i>GbR</i>), <i>BGB-Gesellschaft</i>:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[45]</a></sup> simple partnership; no minimum capital, two or more partners, unlimited liability of partners, no commercial business (<i>Handelsgewerbe</i>) that is not small.
<ul><li><i>nicht-eingetragener Verein</i>: un-incorporated <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">association</a>; non-commercial/idealistic purposes only; similar to <i>e.V.</i></li></ul></li>
<li>commercial partnerships (<i>Personenhandelsgesellschaften</i>)
<ul><li><i>Offene Handelsgesellschaft</i> (<i>OHG</i>): literally "open business company" ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a>: no minimum capital, unlimited liability of partners; GbR with commercial business (<i>Handelsgewerbe</i>)</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">Kommanditgesellschaft</a></i> (<i>KG</i>) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a>
<ul><li>In case the general partner is a limited company, the legal form of the general partner, followed by "<i>&amp; Compagnie</i>" (shortened to <i>&amp; Co.</i>), must be included in the name of the company, resulting in combined legal forms such as:
<ul><li>GmbH &amp; Co. KG: the general partner is a GmbH</li>
<li>AG &amp; Co. KG: the general partner is an AG</li>
<li>GmbH &amp; Co. OHG: each of the general partners are a GmbH</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><i>Partnerschaftsgesellschaft</i> (<i>PartG</i>): partnership company; only for professional services
<ul><li><i>Partnerschaftsgesellschaft mit beschränkter Berufshaftung</i> (<i>PartGmbBH</i>): partnership company with limited professional liability ≈ limited liability partnership (US); only for professional services</li></ul></li>
<li><i>Partenreederei</i>: combined and continued ownership of a single merchant vessel; no longer available for new businesses since 24 April 2013.</li></ul></li>
<li>companies
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Registered_association_(Germany)" title="Registered association (Germany)">eingetragener Verein</a></i> (<i>e.V.</i>): incorporated <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">association</a>; non-commercial/idealistic purposes only, commercial business cannot be the main purpose of the <i>e.V.</i>
<ul><li><i>altrechtlicher Verein</i>/<i>rechtsfähiger Verein</i> (<i>r.V.</i>): <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">association</a> established before 1 January 1900; extremely rare</li>
<li><i>wirtschaftlicher Verein</i>: commercial purpose, established by public grant; rare</li></ul></li>
<li>Companies limited by shares (equity) (<i>Kapitalgesellschaften</i>)
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership#Germany" title="Limited partnership">Kommanditgesellschaft auf Aktien</a></i> (<i>KGaA</i>): ≈ publicly traded partnership (US); although it is a company limited by shares, the KGaA has at least one general partner whose liability is not limited
<ul><li>As with the <i>KG</i>, the legal form of the general partner, followed by "<i>&amp; Compagnie</i>" (shortened to <i>&amp; Co.</i>), must be included if it is another limited company, resulting in combined legal forms such as:
<ul><li>GmbH &amp; Co. KGaA: the general partner is a GmbH</li>
<li>AG &amp; Co. KGaA: the general partner is an AG</li>
<li>SE &amp; Co. KGaA: the general partner is a <i><a href="/wiki/Societas_Europaea" title="Societas Europaea">societas Europaea</a></i></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung</a></i> (<i>GmbH</i>; <small>German: </small><span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[ˈgeːɛmbeːˌhaː]</a></span>): company with limited liability ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">private limited company</a> (<a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a>) (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a> (LLC) (US); at least one shareholder; minimum equity €25,000.
<ul><li>The "mit beschränkter Haftung (mbH)" suffix (<small>German: </small><span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[ˈɛmbeːˌhaː]</a></span>, "with limited liability") is sometimes added to the name of a firm that already ends in "-gesellschaft" ("company"), e.g., "Mustermann Dental-Handelsgesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung" ("dental trading company with limited liability"), which would be abbreviated as "Mustermann Dental-Handelsgesellschaft mbH".</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Entrepreneurial_company_(Germany)" title="Entrepreneurial company (Germany)">Unternehmergesellschaft (haftungsbeschränkt)</a></i> (<i>UG (haftungsbeschränkt)</i>): literally "entrepreneurship company (with limited liability)": identical to <i>GmbH</i> but with a minimum capital of €1 (times the number of shares); part of earnings needs to remain in the company to reach a minimum equity of €25,000; the word <i>haftungsbeschränkt</i> ("with limited liability") may not be abbreviated.</li></ul></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">Aktiengesellschaft</a></i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a></i>): literally "stock company" ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">public limited company</a> (plc) (UK), corporation (US); minimum capital €50,000.</li></ul></li>
<li><i>eingetragene Genossenschaft</i> (<i>e.G.</i>): registered <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li>
<li><i>Körperschaft des öffentlichen Rechts</i>: corporation under public law; main purpose is non-commercial, part of public administration</li></ul></li>
<li>others
<ul><li><i>Stiftung</i> ≈ (private) <a href="/wiki/Private_foundation" title="Private foundation">foundation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trust_law" title="Trust law">trust</a></li>
<li><i>Stiftung des öffentlichen Rechts</i>: foundation under public law; main purpose is non-commercial, part of public administration</li>
<li><i>Anstalt des öffentlichen Rechts</i>: institution under public law; main purpose is non-commercial, part of public administration</li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Greece">Greece</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Greece">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>A.E. (Anónimi Etaireía / Ανώνυμη Εταιρεία, Α.E.; officially translated into <a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), minimum capital €24,000
<ul><li>A.V.E.E. (Anónimi Viomichanikí Emborikí Etaireía / Ανώνυμη Βιομηχανική Εμπορική Εταιρεία, Α.Β.Ε.Ε.)</li></ul></li>
<li>E.E. (Eterórrithmi Etaireía / Ετερόρρυθμη Εταιρία, Ε.Ε.): <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>E.P.E. (Etaireía Periorisménis Efthínis / Εταιρεία Περιορισμένης Ευθύνης, Ε.Π.Ε.): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK), no minimum capital
<ul><li>M.E.P.E. (Monoprósopi Etaireía Periorisménis Efthínis / Μονοπρόσωπη Ε.Π.Ε., Μ.Ε.Π.Ε.): type of E.P.E. with a single member</li></ul></li>
<li>O.E. (Omórrithmi Etaireía / Ομόρρυθμη Εταιρεία, Ο.Ε.): <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a>
<ul><li>O.V.E.E. (Omórrithmi Viomichanikí Emborikí Etaireía / Ομόρρυθμη Βιομηχανική Εμπορική Εταιρεία, Ο.Β.Ε.Ε.)</li></ul></li>
<li>I.K.E. (Idiotiki Kefalaiouchiki Etaireía / Ιδιωτική Κεφαλαιουχική Εταιρεία) = Private Company, minimum capital=€0. The shares do not take the form just of capital but also warranties, labor offer etc. This form is a composite form between A.E. E.P.E and O.E. which is greatly affected by the Articles of Incorporation.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Guatemala">Guatemala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Guatemala">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>y Cía. S. C. (Sociedad Colectiva)</li>
<li>y Cía. S. en C. (Sociedad en Comandita Simple)</li>
<li>Cía. Ltda. (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada)</li>
<li>S. A. (Sociedad Anónima)</li>
<li>Cía. S. C. A (Sociedad en Comandita por Acciones)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Haiti">Haiti</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Haiti">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Standardized Company; Legal Form, Sociedad Anónima (SA) – Stock Corporation; Minimum Capital Requirement, 25,000</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Hong Kong">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Ltd (Limited/有限公司): may denote either a <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">private</a> or <a href="/wiki/Public_company" title="Public company">public company</a> limited by shares, or a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Company_limited_by_guarantee" title="Company limited by guarantee">company limited by guarantee</a>. Under the Companies Ordinance, the name of a Hong Kong incorporated company may be registered in English, Chinese, or both.</li>
<li>Unltd or Ultd (Unlimited/無限公司): similar to a limited liability company (Ltd) but whose members or shareholders do not benefit from limited liability should the company ever go into formal <a href="/wiki/Liquidation" title="Liquidation">liquidation</a>. It is not a requirement under company law to add or state the word or designation Unlimited (無限公司) or its abbreviations (Unltd or Ultd) at the ending of its legal company name, and most <a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">unlimited companies</a> do not.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungary">Hungary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Hungary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In Hungary, business entities are mainly regulated by the Companies Act of 2006,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[46]</a></sup> the Companies Registration Act of 2006 and the new Civil Code of 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48">[47]</a></sup> All companies are required to indicate their type in their name.
</p>

<td>must be a natural person
</td></tr>
<tr>

<td>sole venture</td>
<td>a company registered by and consisting of one sole trader
</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iceland">Iceland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Iceland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
