<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: India">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Indian_company_law" title="Indian company law">Indian company law</a></div>
<ul><li>Sole Proprietorship – A sole proprietorship, also known as a one-person company or proprietorship, is a business firm that is owned and run by one individual. A sole proprietor may use a trade name or business name other than his or her name. Registration not required.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>Partnership – liability is joint and unlimited. Registration not compulsory and can be done through registrar of firms<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
<ul><li>Active partners take part in day-to-day operations of the business, in addition to investing in it. Active partners are entitled to a share of the enterprise's profits.</li>
<li>Sleeping partners invest in the business and are entitled to a share of its profits, but do not participate in day-to-day operations.</li></ul></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Liability_Partnership" title="Limited Liability Partnership">Limited Liability Partnership</a> – Liability is limited and similar to Partnership.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hindu_joint_family" title="Hindu joint family">HUF (Hindu Undivided Family)</a> – businesses owned by a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joint_family" title="Joint family">joint family</a> belonging to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hindu" title="Hindu">Hindu</a> religion. Even though <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jain" title="Jain">Jain</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sikh" title="Sikh">Sikh</a> families are not governed by the Hindu law, they can still form a HUF.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">Cooperative</a></li>
<li>Dormant company – A company which has been created for a future project or for holding assets including intellectual property of the company</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Family_business" title="Family business">Family Owned Business</a></li>
<li>Pvt Ltd (Private Limited Company): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd</a> (UK) – May have 2–200 shareholders; shares are held privately and cannot be offered to public.</li>
<li>Small company – A company other than a public company whose paid up share capital is not more than <span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span> 50 lakh and turnover does not exceed <span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span> crore.</li>
<li>Ltd (Public Limited Company): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Public_sector_undertakings_in_India" title="Public sector undertakings in India">Public sector undertaking (PSU)</a> – Alternatively known as Public Sector Enterprise (PSE). It may be public limited company listed on stock exchanges with major ownership by a state government or a central government of India or it may be unlisted entity with major ownership by a state government or a central government of India. Some of these entities are formed as business entities through special legislation, where these entities are governed by the statutes of these legislation and may or may not be governed by company laws like a typical business entity.</li>
<li>One-person company – It is a type of private company which can have only one director and member.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unlimited_Company" title="Unlimited Company">Unlimited Company</a> – A company, similar to its limited company (Ltd, or Pvt Ltd) counterpart, but where the liability of the members or shareholders is not limited.</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Incorporation_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Incorporation Company (page does not exist)">Incorporation Company</a> – Incorporation is the formation of a new corporation. The corporation may be a business, a non-profit organization, sports club, or a government of a new city or town.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesia">Indonesia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Indonesia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Most of the legal entity types are regulated in a modified version of the original version of the Dutch <i><a href="/wiki/Burgerlijk_Wetboek" title="Burgerlijk Wetboek">Burgerlijk Wetboek</a></i>.
</p>
<ul><li><i>Yayasan</i>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foundation_(nonprofit_organization)" title="Foundation (nonprofit organization)">foundation</a></li>
<li>UD (<a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">Indonesian</a>: <i lang="id">Usaha Dagang</i>): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (lit. "trade company").
<ul><li>Sometimes this kind of legal entity is called a <i>perusahaan dagang</i> or abbreviated as PD, which sometimes makes confusion with the former name for municipally-owned statutory corporations, <i>Perusahaan Daerah</i>, also abbreviated as PD (today they are called <i>Perusahaan Umum Daerah</i> ("regional public corporations") and abbreviated as <i>Perumda</i>)</li></ul></li>
<li>vof/Fa (<a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>: <i lang="nl">vennootschap onder firma</i>), known locally as just <i>firma</i>: <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>Koperasi: <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">Cooperative</a></li>
<li>mts (maatschap) (<a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">Indonesian</a>: <i lang="id">Persekutuan Perdata</i>): ≈ group practice (of professionals, e.g. doctors, accountants, lawyers); share facilities not profits, members are treated as natural persons for tax and liability purposes.</li>
<li>cv (<a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>: <i lang="nl">Commanditaire vennootschap</i>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">Indonesian</a>: <i lang="id">Perusahaan/Persekutuan Komanditer</i>) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">LP</a> (US), <a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">Kommanditgesellschaft</a> (Germany); a more common type for smaller businesses</li>
<li>PT (<a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">Indonesian</a>: <i lang="id">Perseroan Terbatas</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">private company limited by shares</a> (UK)
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/State-owned_enterprises_of_Indonesia" title="State-owned enterprises of Indonesia">State-owned</a> PT (both in majority and complete ownership) ends with "(<i>Persero</i>)".</li></ul></li>
<li>PT Tbk (Perseroan Terbatas Terbuka or Perseroan Terbuka) (also in <a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>: <i lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/Naamloze_vennootschap" title="Naamloze vennootschap">Naamloze vennootschap</a></i>, NV): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) listed on the <a href="/wiki/Indonesia_Stock_Exchange" title="Indonesia Stock Exchange">Indonesia Stock Exchange</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iran">Iran</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Iran">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>شرکت سهامی عام (<i>Sherkat Sahami Am</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), public</li>
<li>شرکت سهامی خاص (<i>Sherkat Sahami Khas</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), private</li>
<li>شرکت با مسئولیت محدود (<i>Sherkat ba Masouliyat Mahdoud</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>شرکت مختلط غیر سهامی (<i>Sherkat Mokhtalet Gheyr Sahami</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>شرکت مختلط سهامی (<i>Sherkat Mokhtalet Sahami</i>): mixed joint-stock partnership</li>
<li>شرکت تضامنی (<i>Sherkat Tazamoni</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>شرکت نسبی (<i>Sherkat Nesbi</i>): proportional liability partnership</li>
<li>شرکت تعاونی تولید و مصرف (<i>Sherkat Ta'avoni Tolid va Masraf</i>): production and consumption cooperative</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ireland">Ireland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Ireland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Situation in <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a> is similar to <a href="#United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> below, though without the class <i>Community Interest Company</i>. There were two forms of Company Limited by Guarantee, but only the form <i>without a share capital</i> is now used. <a href="/wiki/Irish_language" title="Irish language">Irish</a> names may also be used, such as <i>cpt</i> (<i lang="ga" title="Irish language text">cuideachta phoibli theoranta</i>) for plc, and <i>Teo</i> (Teoranta) for Ltd.
</p>
<ul><li>Limited Company – Four types:
<ul><li>Private company limited by shares – If company is wound up, members' liability is limited to the amount, if any, unpaid on the shares they hold. Maximum number of members in the Republic of Ireland is 99.</li>
<li>Company limited by guarantee not having a share capital – Public company. Must have at least seven members. Members' liability limited to amount they have undertaken to contribute to company assets. If wound up, liability does not exceed amount specified in memorandum. If a guarantee company does not have a share capital, members are not required to buy shares (such as charities).</li>
<li>Company limited by guarantee having a share capital – As with a private company if the maximum number of members is 99. Members have liability either for the amount, if any, that is unpaid on the shares they hold, or for the amount they have undertaken to contribute to company assets, in the event that it is wound up.</li>
<li>A public limited company. Must have at least seven members. Liability is limited to the amount, if any, unpaid on shares they hold. Unlawful to issue any form of prospectus except in compliance with the Companies Acts 1963–2006. Nominal value of Company's allotted share capital must satisfy specified minimums which must be fully paid before company commences business or exercises any borrowing powers.</li></ul></li>
<li>Single Member Company – Private company limited by shares or a guarantee company having a share capital, which is incorporated with one member, or whose membership is reduced to one person. Must have at least two directors and one secretary. Sole member can dispense with holding General Meetings including Annual General Meetings.</li>
<li>Unlimited Company – No limit on liability of members. Creditors may have recourse to shareholders for unpaid liabilities of the company. Must have at least two shareholders.</li>
<li>Undertakings for Collective Investment in Transferable Securities (UCITS) – Public limited companies formed under EU Regulation and the Companies Acts 1963–2006. Sole object of a UCIT is collective investment in transferable securities of capital raised from the public that operates on the principle of risk-spreading. Central Bank of Ireland must approve all registrations of UCITS.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Israel">Israel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Israel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Company (<i>khevra</i>, חברה) – for-profit entity which may engage in any lawful activity. Most companies limit the liability of their shareholders. In that case, the phrase "Limited" or the abbreviation "Ltd." must appear as part of the full name of the company. The term "B.M."/"BM" (בע"מ), literally: by limited liability/warranty, is usually translated as "Ltd." in English and pronounced "ba'AM" in Hebrew. Companies are governed by the Companies Act, 5759-1999 (חוק החברות, תשנ"ט-1999). Few sections are still in force from the Companies Ordinance [New Form], 5743-1983 (פקודת החברות [נוסח חדש], תשמ"ג-1983).
<ul><li>Private company – any company which is not a public company.</li>
<li>Public company – any company whose shares are listed on an exchange or have been offered to the public, and are held by the public.</li>
<li>Charity company (<i>khevra le'to'ellet ha'tzibur</i>, חברה לתועלת הציבור) – company generally governed by the Companies Act, except it is a nonprofit. A charity company must have pre-defined goals, rather than engage in any lawful activity. Some provisions in the Companies Act apply specifically to charity companies. The letters "CC" (חל"צ) must be appended to such company's name.</li></ul></li>
<li>Partnership (<i>shutafut</i>, שותפות) – created by default, even without registration, when two or more persons run a business together for profit. Personal liability of partners is not limited, unless they are limited partners of a limited partnership. Partnerships are governed by the Partnerships Ordinance [New Form], 5735-1975 (פקודת השותפויות [נוסח חדש], תשל"ה-1975).</li>
<li>Cooperative (<i>aguda shitufit</i>, אגודה שיתופית) – entity which may pursue profit, but with certain legal properties meant to facilitate greater participation by each shareholder, or member, in the entity's affairs. Shareholders usually have an additional relationship with the cooperative, such as employees or consumers. This type of entity is found mainly in agriculture (a <a href="/wiki/Kibbutz" title="Kibbutz">kibbutz</a> or <a href="/wiki/Moshav" title="Moshav">moshav</a> is often a cooperative), transportation, or certain types of marketing operations associated with agricultural products. Cooperatives are governed by the Cooperatives Ordinance (פקודת האגודות השיתופיות).</li>
<li>Voluntary association (<i>amuta</i>, עמותה) – nonprofit entity, which must have its goals defined in its founding agreement. Includes, among others, academic institutions, hospitals and various charitable organizations. Voluntary associations are governed by the Voluntary Associations Act, 5740-1980 (חוק העמותות, תש"מ-1980).</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Italy">Italy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Italy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Forme individuali</i> (Individuals):
<ul><li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Artigiano</i> (Artisan)</li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Lavoratore autonomo</i> (Independent worker)</li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Libero professionista</i> (<a href="/wiki/Professional" title="Professional">Professional</a>)</li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Imprenditore</i> ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_trader" title="Sole trader">sole trader</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (US)</li></ul></li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società di persone</i> (Partnerships):
<ul><li>S.s. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società semplice</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> (non commercial)</li>
<li>S.n.c. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società in nome collettivo</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> (commercial)</li>
<li>S.a.s. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società in accomandita semplice</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li></ul></li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società di capitali</i> (Companies):
<ul><li>S.p.a. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text"><a href="/wiki/Societ%C3%A0_per_azioni" title="Società per azioni">Società per azioni</a></i>):<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[50]</a></sup> ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a> (US)</li>
<li>S.a.p.a. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società in accomandita per azioni</i>): ≈ publicly traded partnership</li>
<li>S.c.p.a. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società consortile per azioni</i>)</li>
<li>S.c.a.r.l. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società consortile a responsabilità limitata</i>)</li>
<li>S.r.l. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text"><a href="/wiki/Societ%C3%A0_a_responsabilit%C3%A0_limitata" title="Società a responsabilità limitata">Società a responsabilità limitata</a></i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US)</li></ul></li>
<li><i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Cooperative</i> (Cooperatives):
<ul><li>S.c.r.l. (<i lang="it" title="Italian language text">Società cooperativa a responsabilità limitata</i>) <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a> limited (liability) company</li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Japan">Japan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Japan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Business corporations are referred to as <i>kaisha</i> (会社) and are formed under the <a href="/wiki/Law_of_Japan" title="Law of Japan">Companies Act</a> of 2005. There are currently (2015) 4 types and each of them has legal personality:
</p>
<ul><li>株式会社 (<i><a href="/wiki/Kabushiki_gaisha" title="Kabushiki gaisha">kabushiki gaisha</a></i> or <i>kabushiki kaisha</i>, "K.K." (usually translated in company names as "Company, Limited"/"Co., Ltd.")) – lit. "stock company", the most typical form of business corporation.</li>
<li>合同会社 (<i><a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dd%C5%8D_gaisha" title="Gōdō gaisha">gōdō gaisha</a></i> or <i>gōdō kaisha</i>, "G.K.") – lit. "amalgamated company", a close corporation form similar to the American LLC, introduced in 2006
<ul><li>有限会社 (<i><a href="/wiki/Y%C5%ABgen_gaisha" title="Yūgen gaisha">yūgen gaisha</a></i> or <i>yūgen kaisha</i>, "Y.K.") – lit. "limited company", a close corporation form for smaller businesses, abolished in 2006 and replaced by G.K. above</li></ul></li>
<li>合名会社 (<i><a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dmei_gaisha" title="Gōmei gaisha">gōmei gaisha</a></i> or <i>gōmei kaisha</i>, "GMK") – corporation similar to a general partnership</li>
<li>合資会社 (<i><a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dshi_gaisha" title="Gōshi gaisha">gōshi gaisha</a></i> or <i>gōshi kaisha</i>, "GSK") – corporation similar to a limited partnership</li></ul>
<p>Partnerships are referred to as <i>kumiai</i> (組合). Each of these 4 types has no legal personality though other corporations, which include "<i>kumiai</i>" in their name, have:
</p>
<ul><li>任意組合 (<i>nin'i kumiai</i>, "NK") – general partnership (Civil Code)</li>
<li>匿名組合 (<i><a href="/wiki/Tokumei_kumiai" title="Tokumei kumiai">tokumei kumiai</a></i>, "TK") – anonymous partnership, an investment bilateral contract (Commercial Code, Book 2 Ch.4 Article 535 et seq)</li>
<li>投資事業有限責任組合 (<i><a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership#Japan" title="Limited partnership">tōshi jigyō yūgen sekinin kumiai</a></i>) – limited partnership for investment (Limited Partnership for Investment Act 1998, Rev.2004)</li>
<li>有限責任事業組合 (<i><a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">yūgen sekinin jigyō kumiai</a></i>) – similar to a Limited Liability Partnership (Limited Liability Partnership Act of 2005)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Jordan">Jordan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Jordan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Partnership (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=General_Partnership_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="General Partnership Company (page does not exist)">General Partnership Company</a></i>).</li>
<li>Limited Liability (<i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Liability_Company" title="Limited Liability Company">Limited Liability Company</a></i>).</li>
<li>Limited Liability in Shares (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Limited_Liability_in_Shares&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Limited Liability in Shares (page does not exist)">Limited Liability in Shares</a></i>).</li>
<li>Public Shareholding (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Public_listed_stock_company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Public listed stock company (page does not exist)">Public listed stock company</a></i>).</li>
<li>Private Shareholding Companies (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Private_listed_stock_company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Private listed stock company (page does not exist)">Private listed stock company</a></i>).</li>
<li>Foreign Company (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Non-Jordanian_company_operating_in_Jordan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Non-Jordanian company operating in Jordan (page does not exist)">Non-Jordanian company operating in Jordan</a></i>).</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Kazakhstan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>АО (Aktsionernoe obschestvo/<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%90%D0%BA%D1%86%D0%B8%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BE%D0%B1%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Акционерное общество (page does not exist)">Акционерное общество</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%90%D0%BA%D1%86%D0%B8%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BE%D0%B1%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE" title="ru:Акционерное общество">ru</a>]</sup>): Joint stock company</li>
<li>ТОО (Tovarishchestvo s ogranichennoy otvetstvennostyu/<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE_%D1%81_%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B8%D1%87%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C%D1%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Товарищество с ограниченной ответственностью (page does not exist)">Товарищество с ограниченной ответственностью</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE_%D1%81_%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B8%D1%87%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C%D1%8E" title="ru:Товарищество с ограниченной ответственностью">ru</a>]</sup>): limited liability partnership</li>
<li>TDO/ТДО (Tovarishchestvo s dopolnitelnoyu otvetstvennostyu/Товарищество с дополнительной ответственностью) Additional liability partnership</li>
<li>GP/ГП (Gosudarstvenoe predpriyatie/<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%93%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%83%D0%B4%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%8F%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Государственное предприятие (page does not exist)">Государственное предприятие</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%93%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%83%D0%B4%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%8F%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%B5" title="ru:Государственное предприятие">ru</a>]</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[51]</a></sup>): State company</li>
<li>КТ (Komanditnoe Tovarishchestvo; Командитное товарищество)</li>
<li>ОО (Obshestvennoe Obedinenie / Общественное объединение) Social association</li>
<li>PT/ПТ (Polnoe Tovarishchestvo / Полное товарищество) Full partnership</li>
<li>PtK/ПтК (Potrebibitelskii Kooperativ / Потребительский кооператив)</li>
<li>PrK/ПрК (Proizvodstvenni Kooperativ / Производственный кооператив)</li>
<li>РО (Relitioznoe Obedinenie / Религиозное объединение)</li>
<li>Uchr/Учр (Uchrezhdenie/Учреждение)</li></ul>
<h2><span id="Korea.2C_South"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Korea,_South">Korea, South</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Korea, South">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>South Korea's legal entity types are a remnant from Japanese occupation.
</p>
<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%EC%A3%BC%EC%8B%9D%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="주식회사 (page does not exist)">주식회사</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%EC%A3%BC%EC%8B%9D%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC" title="ko:주식회사">ko</a>]</sup> or 株式會社 (<i>jusik hoesa</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Kabushiki_gaisha" title="Kabushiki gaisha">kabushiki gaisha</a> (Japan); <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%EC%9C%A0%ED%95%9C%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="유한회사 (page does not exist)">유한회사</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%EC%9C%A0%ED%95%9C%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC" title="ko:유한회사">ko</a>]</sup> or 有限會社 (<i>yuhan hoesa</i>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Y%C5%ABgen_gaisha" title="Yūgen gaisha">yūgen gaisha</a>/<a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dd%C5%8D_gaisha" title="Gōdō gaisha">gōdō gaisha</a> (Japan); <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a> (UK); <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GmbH" title="GmbH">GmbH</a> (Germany)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%EC%9C%A0%ED%95%9C%EC%B1%85%EC%9E%84%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="유한책임회사 (page does not exist)">유한책임회사</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%EC%9C%A0%ED%95%9C%EC%B1%85%EC%9E%84%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC" title="ko:유한책임회사">ko</a>]</sup> or 有限責任會社 (<i>yuhan chaeg-im hoesa</i>): <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a>; ≈ <a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dd%C5%8D_gaisha" title="Gōdō gaisha">gōdō gaisha</a> (Japan)</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%ED%95%A9%EC%9E%90%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="합자회사 (page does not exist)">합자회사</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%ED%95%A9%EC%9E%90%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC" title="ko:합자회사">ko</a>]</sup> or 合資會社 (<i>hapja hoesa</i>): <a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dshi_gaisha" title="Gōshi gaisha">gōshi gaisha</a> (Japan); corporation similar to a <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%ED%95%A9%EB%AA%85%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="합명회사 (page does not exist)">합명회사</a><sup class="noprint" style="font-style: normal;"> [<a class="extiw" href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%ED%95%A9%EB%AA%85%ED%9A%8C%EC%82%AC" title="ko:합명회사">ko</a>]</sup> or 合名會社 (<i>hapmyeong hoesa</i>): <a href="/wiki/G%C5%8Dmei_gaisha" title="Gōmei gaisha">gōmei gaisha</a> (Japan); corporation similar to a <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Latvia">Latvia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Latvia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SIA (Sabiedrība ar ierobežotu atbildību): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>AS (<a href="/wiki/Akciju_sabiedr%C4%ABba" title="Akciju sabiedrība">Akciju sabiedrība</a>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>IK (Individuālais komersants): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>PS (Pilnsabiedrība) ≈ general partnership, joint venture</li>
<li>KS (Komandītsabiedrība): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>ĀKF (Ārzemju komersanta filiāle): branch of a foreign enterprise</li>
<li>BO (Bezpeļņas organizācija): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Nonprofit_organization" title="Nonprofit organization">nonprofit organization</a></li>
<li>VSIA (Valsts sabiedrība ar ierobežotu atbildību): ≈ state-owned <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lebanon">Lebanon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Lebanon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Soci%C3%A9t%C3%A9_anonyme_libanaise" title="Société anonyme libanaise">s.a.l.</a> (Societe Anonyme Libanaise): a form of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joint_stock_company" title="Joint stock company">joint stock company</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A0rl" title="Sàrl">S.A.R.L.</a> (Société à responsabilité limitée): a form of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Liability_Company" title="Limited Liability Company">Limited Liability Company</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Partnership" title="Partnership">Partnership</a></li></ul>
<ol><li>S.N.C.(Société en Nom Collectif): General partnership</li>
<li>S.C.S.(Société en Commandite Simple): Partnership in commendam</li></ol>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holding_Company" title="Holding Company">Holding Company</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Offshore_company" title="Offshore company">Offshore company</a>RR</li>
<li>Branch of Foreign Company</li>
<li>Representative Office</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lithuania">Lithuania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Lithuania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>UAB (Uždaroji akcinė bendrovė): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>AB (Akcinė bendrovė): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>VšĮ (Viešoji įstaiga): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-profit_organization" title="Non-profit organization">non-profit organization</a></li>
<li>IĮ (Individuali įmonė): ≈ personal enterprise</li>
<li>Individuali veikla = <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (does not possess legal personality of its own)</li>
<li>TŪB (Tikroji ūkinė bendrija): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>KŪB (Komanditinė ūkinė bendrija): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>MB (Mažoji bendrija) : ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Limited liabilityCGT partnership</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Luxembourg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Société anonyme): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A0rl" title="Sàrl">S.A.R.L.</a> (Société à responsabilité limitée): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>Société à responsabilité limitée simplifiée (SARL-S) = simplified limited liability company</li>
<li>Société en commandite simple (SCS): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>Société en Commandite Spéciale (SCSp): unlike an SCS, an SCSp does not have a legal personality separate from those of its partners; it is formed by an agreement among its partners and allows for more flexible structuring, not having to comply with corporate law requirements</li>
<li>Société en commandite par actions (SCA): ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Corporate_limited_partnership&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Corporate limited partnership (page does not exist)">corporate limited partnership</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malaysia">Malaysia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Malaysia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Perkongsian_Liabiliti_Terhad&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Perkongsian Liabiliti Terhad (page does not exist)">PLT</a> (Perkongsian Liabiliti Terhad): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Liability_Partnership" title="Limited Liability Partnership">LLP</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Berhad" title="Berhad">Bhd.</a> (Berhad): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sendirian_Berhad" title="Sendirian Berhad">Sdn. Bhd.</a> (Sendirian Berhad): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">Mexico</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Mexico">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dt>Business entities according to the "Ley General de Sociedades Mercantiles" (General Law of Business entities)</dt></dl>
<ul><li>Persona Física</li>
<li>S.A. (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sociedad_An%C3%B3nima" title="Sociedad Anónima">Sociedad Anónima</a>): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>S. de R.L.(Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>Associates name and "y compañía" or Associates name and "y sucesores"(Sociedad en Nombre Colectivo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>S. en C. (Sociedad en Comandita Simple): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>S. en C. por A. (Sociedad en Comandita por Acciones): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Master_limited_partnership" title="Master limited partnership">master limited partnership</a></li></ul>
<p>Note: Any of these entities can be incorporated as a "Capital Variable" entity, in which case has to add the "de C.V." sufix to its company name. Example: "S.A. de C.V.", "S. de R.L. de C.V."
</p>
<dl><dt>Business entities according to the "Ley del Mercado de Valores" (Stock Market Law)</dt></dl>
<ul><li>S.A.B. (Sociedad Anónima Bursátil)</li>
<li>S.A.P.I. (Sociedad Anónima Promotora de Inversión)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Monaco">Monaco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Monaco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SAM (Société Anonyme Monégasque): ≈ joint stock company</li>
<li>SARL (Société à Responsabilité Limitée): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_company" title="Limited company">Ltd.</a> (UK), LLC (USA)</li>
<li>SNC (Societe en Nom Collectif): ≈ General Partnership</li>
<li>SCS (Societe En Commandite Simple): ≈ Limited Partnership</li>
<li>SCA (Société en Commandite par Actions): ≈ Limited Partnership with Shares</li>
<li>Sole Trader</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mongolia">Mongolia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Mongolia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>ХК (Khuvitsaat Kompani/Хувьцаат Компани): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) stock company</li>
<li>ХХК (Khyazgaarlagdmal Khariutslagatai Kompani/ Хязгаарлагдмал Хариуцлагатай Компани): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">ltd</a> (UK) limited liability company</li>
<li>ТББ (Töriin Bus Baiguullaga/Төрийн Бус Байгууллага):≈ non governmental organisation</li>
<li>ГХО ХХК (Gadaadiin khurungu oruulalttai khyazgaarlagdmal khariutslagatai kompani / Гадаадын хөрөнгө оруулалттай хязгаарлагдмал хариуцлагатай компани): ≈ limited liability company with foreign investment</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Montenegro">Montenegro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Montenegro">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Preduzetnik        (Preduzetnik):                         ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a> (UK)                                 ≈ Einzelunternehmen/Eingetragener Kaufmann (D)</li>
<li>O.D. (Ortačko Društvo):                     ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a> (UK)                                 ≈ Offene Handelsgesellschaft ≈ OHG (D)</li>
<li>K.D. (Komanditno Društvo):                  ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">Limited partnership</a> (UK)                                 ≈ <a href="/wiki/Kommanditgesellschaft" title="Kommanditgesellschaft">KG</a> (D)</li>
<li>A.D. (Akcionarsko Društvo):                 ≈ <a href="/wiki/Joint-stock_company" title="Joint-stock company">joint-stock company</a>, <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (D)</li>
<li>D.O.O. (Društvo sa Ograničenom Odgovornošću): ≈ Private Limited Companies (Ltd.) (UK)                        ≈ <a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">GmbH</a> (D)</li>
<li>Dio stranog društva (Dio stranog društva):
<ul><li>Literally <i>part of a foreign company</i> this sort of business entity contains the original name, legal organizational form from origin country which is converted in</li></ul></li></ul>
<p>one of above mentioned form (Preduzetnik; O.D.; K.D.; A.D.; D.O.O.), as such it is registered in the Central Register of Companies. This form is a little bit specific and was created for companies that are domiciled registered in other countries and have its part in Montenegro.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Morocco">Morocco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Morocco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>S.A (Société Anonyme): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Public_Limited_Company" title="Public Limited Company">Public Limited Company</a> (P.L.C) (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corporation</a> (US/Can)</li>
<li>S.A.S (Société Anonyme Simplifiée): ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Unlisted_Public_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Unlisted Public Company (page does not exist)">Unlisted Public Company</a> (Au), <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Close_Corporation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Close Corporation (page does not exist)">Close Corporation</a> (CC) (S. Africa), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Private_Corporation" title="Private Corporation">Private Corporation</a> (Can); often used for subsidiaries; minimum of one director and two members/shareholders; no limit on share capital; liability can be restricted to director; no "one share – one vote" principle</li>
<li>S.A.R.L (Société à Responsabilité Limitée): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Private_Limited_company" title="Private Limited company">Private Limited company</a> (Ltd.) (UK), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Liability_Company" title="Limited Liability Company">Limited Liability Company</a> (US)</li>
<li>G.I.E (Groupement d'Intérêt Economique): economic interest grouping</li>
<li>S.N.C (Société en Nom Collectif): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Partnership" title="General Partnership">General Partnership</a> (GP)</li>
<li>S.C.S (Société en Commandite Simple): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Limited_Partnership" title="Limited Partnership">Limited Partnership</a> (LP)</li>
<li>S.C.A (Société en Commandite par Actions): ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Publicly_Traded_Partnership&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Publicly Traded Partnership (page does not exist)">Publicly Traded Partnership</a> (PTP) (US)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Namibia">Namibia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Namibia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Close Corporation*</li>
<li>Companies (Private, Public and Section 21)*</li>
<li>Sole Trader*</li>
<li>Partnership*</li>
<li>Trusts*</li>
<li>Co-operatives*</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nepal">Nepal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Nepal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Private Limited Company: Liability, limited by shares; Name, cannot be deceptively similar to another registered company; Management, at least 1 director; Shareholders, limited to 1–50 excluding persons who are employed by company, prohibition against any invitation to the public to subscribe for shares; Founders, 1–50; Nationality, Nepalese company; Company purpose, any lawful purpose except industry on Negative List; Formation, file Memorandum and Articles of Association with Registrar of Companies.</li>
<li>Public Limited Company: Liability, limited by shares; Name, cannot be deceptively similar to another registered company; Management, at least 3 directors; Shareholders, minimum 7, no maximum, share subscription by public pursuant to a prospectus that complies with Companies Act of 2007 and Securities Act; a Private Limited Company can convert to Public Limited Company by complying with Companies Act of 2007; Founders, minimum 7; Nationality, Nepalese company; Company purpose, any lawful purpose except industry on Negative List; Formation, file Memorandum and Articles of Association with Registrar of Companies.</li>
<li>Branch: Liability, main company remains liable; Name, same as main company; Nationality, foreign company; Company purpose, any lawful purpose except industry on Negative List; Formation, file Memorandum and Articles of Association with Registrar of Companies, plus permission to work in Nepal by concerned authority; Founders, main branch.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands">Netherlands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Netherlands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Stichting" title="Stichting">Stichting</a>: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foundation_(non-profit)" title="Foundation (non-profit)">foundation</a>. Can run a business. No profit distribution to founders or board members.</li>
<li><i>mutual societies</i> (associations which are allowed to pay dividends to their members; liability may be unlimited (W.A. – Wettelijke Aansprakelijkheid), limited (B.A. – Beperkte Aansprakelijkheid) or exempt (U.A. – Uitsluiting van Aansprakelijkheid)):
<ul><li>Coöperatie: ≈ co-operative society</li>
<li>Onderlinge waarborgmaatschappij: ≈ mutual insurance company</li></ul></li>
<li>Mij (Maatschappij): ≈ association</li>
<li>Mts (Maatschap): ≈ group practice (of professionals, e.g. doctors, accountants, lawyers); share facilities not profits, members are treated as natural persons for tax and liability purposes.</li>
<li>Eenmanszaak: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_trader" title="Sole trader">sole trader</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (US)</li>
<li><i>incorporated entities</i>:
<ul><li>vof (Vennootschap onder firma): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">GP</a></li>
<li>cv (Commanditaire vennootschap): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">LP</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Besloten_vennootschap" title="Besloten vennootschap">bv</a> (Besloten vennootschap): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US). Shares are privately registered and not freely transferable. The name means "closed company", stemming from the fact that the (group of) shareholder(s) is cannot be changed without consent from the majority of shareholder(s).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Naamloze_vennootschap" title="Naamloze vennootschap">nv</a> (Naamloze vennootschap): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corp.</a> (US). Minimum issued share capital upon incorporation: €45,000. Literally translated, the title has the "nameless company", owing to the fact that shareholders are not formally known as such in company statutes and other legal documents.</li></ul></li></ul>
<p>Companies are registered on the Companies Register and with a regional <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Commerce" title="Chamber of Commerce">Chamber of Commerce</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[52]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: New Zealand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Ltd (Limited): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Names of limited liability companies that were registered under the Companies Act 1993 (but not those that were registered under the Companies Act 1955) must end with the word "Limited", the words "Tāpui (Limited)", or the suffix "Ltd".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Look-through_company" title="Look-through company">Look-through company</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Nicaragua">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Commercial Code establishes the following types of companies:
</p>
<ul><li>S.A.: Sociedad Anónima</li>
<li>Cia.: Sociedad en Nombre Colectivo</li>
<li>Cia. Ltda.: Sociedad en Nombre Colectivo de Responsabilidad Limitada</li>
<li>S.C.S.: Sociedad en Comandita Simple</li>
<li>S.C.A.: Sociedad en Comandita por Acciones</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nigeria">Nigeria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Nigeria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Private Limited Company</a> (Ltd.): a private company limited by shares</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">Public Limited Company</a> (PLC): a public company limited by shares</li>
<li>Limited by Guarantee (Ltd./Gte.): a company limited by guarantee (non-profit company)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">Unlimited</a> (ULtd.): A company with a share capital, similar to its limited company (Ltd., or PLC.) counterparts, but where the liability of the members or shareholders is not limited</li>
<li>Limited Liability Partnership (LLP): Only allowed in the state of Lagos, Nigeria.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Macedonia">North Macedonia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: North Macedonia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>A.D./А.Д. (Akcionersko Društvo / Акционерско друштво): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) or <a href="/wiki/Joint-stock_company" title="Joint-stock company">Joint-stock company</a></li>
<li>D.O.O./Д.О.О. (Društvo so Ograničena Odgovornost / Друштво со ограничена одговорност): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>D.O.O.E.L./Д.О.О.Е.Л. (Društvo so Ograničena Odgovornost od Edno Lice / Друштво со ограничена одговорност основано од едно лице): type of DOO with a single member</li>
<li>K.D./К.Д. (Komanditno Društvo / Командитно друштво): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>K.D.A./К.Д.А. (Komanditno Društvo so Akcie / Командитно друштво со акции): ≈ limited partnership with shares</li>
<li>J.T.D./Ј.Т.Д. (Javno Trgovsko Društvo / Јавно трговско друштво): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norway">Norway</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Norway">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Allmennaksjeselskap" title="Allmennaksjeselskap">ASA</a> (Allmennaksjeselskap): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum capital <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_krone" title="Norwegian krone">NOK</a> 1,000,000</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aksjeselskap" title="Aksjeselskap">AS</a> (Aksjeselskap): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Minimum capital NOK 30,000.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ansvarlig_selskap" title="Ansvarlig selskap">ANS</a> (Ansvarlig selskap): <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> with mutual liability</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Selskap_med_begrenset_ansvar" title="Selskap med begrenset ansvar">BA</a> (Selskap med begrenset ansvar): cooperatives and companies created by legislation</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Borettslag" title="Borettslag">BL</a> (Borettslag): housing share company</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Selskap_med_delt_ansvar" title="Selskap med delt ansvar">DA</a> (Selskap med delt ansvar): general partnership with apportioned liability</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Enkeltpersonforetak" title="Enkeltpersonforetak">Enkeltpersonforetak</a>: sole proprietorship</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Etat" title="Etat">Etat</a>: state, county or municipal agency</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kommunalt_foretak" title="Kommunalt foretak">FKF</a> (Fylkeskommunalt foretak): county enterprise</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Health_Trust" title="Health Trust">HF</a> (helseforetak): subsidiary health enterprise</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Interkommunalt_selskap" title="Interkommunalt selskap">IKS</a> (Interkommunalt selskap): inter-municipal enterprise (owners' liability)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kommunalt_foretak" title="Kommunalt foretak">KF</a> (Kommunalt foretak): municipal enterprise (owner's liability)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kommandittselskap" title="Kommandittselskap">KS</a> (Kommandittselskap): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Norskregistrert_utenlandsk_foretak" title="Norskregistrert utenlandsk foretak">NUF</a> (Norskregistrert utenlandsk foretak): foreign enterprise registered in Norway</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Regional_health_authority_(Norway)" title="Regional health authority (Norway)">RHF</a> (regionalt helseforetak): regional health enterprise</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Statsforetak" title="Statsforetak">SF</a> (Statsforetak): state enterprise</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sparebank" title="Sparebank">Sparebank</a>: savings bank</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stiftelse" title="Stiftelse">Stiftelse</a>: a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foundation_(nonprofit_organization)" title="Foundation (nonprofit organization)">foundation</a>, with capital but without members or shareholders. It is allowed to make a profit, but is more suited for non-commercial purposes.</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ungdomsbedrift&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ungdomsbedrift (page does not exist)">UB</a> (Ungdomsbedrift): youth enterprise, only used in education</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Oman">Oman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Oman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>SAOG (Société Anonyme Omanaise Générale) Public Joint Stock Company<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>SAOC (Société Anonyme Omanaise Close) Closed Joint Stock Company<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[54]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan">Pakistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Pakistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There are three main forms of business:
</p><p>(a) Sole Proprietorship
(b) Partnership
(c) Company
</p>
<ul><li>Sole Proprietorship</li></ul>
<p>In a sole proprietorship, an individual on his/her own account carries out the business or profession. No formal procedure or formality is required for setting up a sole proprietary concern.
</p>
<ul><li>Partnership</li></ul>
<p>A partnership is a business relationship entered into by a formal agreement between two or more persons or corporations carrying on a business in common. The capital for a partnership is provided by the partners who are liable for the total debts of the firms and who share the profits and losses of the business concern according to the terms of the partnership agreement.
</p><p>Partnerships (other than banking companies) are generally limited in size to twenty partners. The interest of a partner is transferable only with the prior consent of the other partner(s). However, a partner's right to a share of the partnership income may be received in trust for another person.
</p><p>For taxation purposes, partnerships are classified into:
</p><p>(i) Registered Firms
(ii) Unregistered Firms
</p><p>The income of the registered firm is subject to Super Tax before distribution to the partners. Also the individual income of the partners is subject to income tax at the usual rates.
</p><p>For unregistered firms, income tax is levied on the firm's income and the partners are not liable to pay tax on the shares of profit received from the unregistered firm(s).
</p>
<ul><li>Company</li></ul>
<p>A company is a legal entity formed under the Companies Ordinance, 1984. It can have share capital or can be formed without share capital.
</p><p>A company having share capital may be formed as:
</p><p>(i) A company limited by shares.
(ii) A company limited by guarantee.
(iii) An unlimited company.
</p>
<ul><li>Company Limited by Shares</li></ul>
<p>The liability of its members is limited to the extent of their shares in the paid-up capital of the company. These companies may further be classified as public limited and private limited companies.
</p>
<ul><li>Public Limited Companies can be formed by at least seven persons by subscribing their names to the 'Memorandum and Articles of Association' of the company. The word 'Limited' is used as the last word of its name.</li>
<li>Private Limited Companies may be formed by at least two persons by subscribing their names to the 'Memorandum and Articles of Association' of the company. A private limited company, by its Articles of Association:</li></ul>
<p>(i) Restricts the right to transfer its shares;
(ii) Limits the number of its members to fifty; and;
(iii) Prohibits any invitation to the public to subscribe for shares or debentures of the company.
</p><p>A private limited company is required to use the words "(Private) Limited" as the last words of its name.
</p>
<ul><li>Company Limited By Guarantee</li></ul>
<p>Means a company having the liability of its members limited by memorandum to such amounts as the members may respectively undertake to contribute to the capital of the company in the event of its winding up. A company limited by guarantee is usually formed on a 'non profit basis'. Companies limited by guarantee use the words (Guarantee) Limited" as the last words of their n
Unlimited Company
</p><p>Means a company having unlimited liability of its members
</p><p><a class="external text" href="https://www.secp.gov.pk" rel="nofollow">https://www.secp.gov.pk</a>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Peru">Peru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Peru">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>Sociedad Anónima Abierta (S.A.A.): To qualify to register as an S.A.A., a company must meet one or more conditions laid down in Article 249 of Peru's General Corporation Law. Those conditions state there must be a primary public offering of shares or convertible bonds in stocks, which are held by more than 750 shareholders, more than 35% of its capital belonging to 175 shareholders, or that all shareholders entitled to vote approve the adjustment to the scheme. The S.A.A. is then audited by the Comisión Nacional Supervisora de Empresas y Valores (CONASEV).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[55]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sociedad Anónima Cerrada (S.A.C.):<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[56]</a></sup> These companies must have a minimum of 2 and a maximum of 20 shareholders. These shares can't be registered in the Public Registry.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">Philippines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Philippines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Co. (Company): can be used for <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnerships</a></li>
<li>Coop. (Cooperative)</li>
<li>Corp. (Corporation)</li>
<li>Ent. (Enterprise): May be used by <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorships</a>, although they are not required to have a suffix.</li>
<li>Inc. (Incorporated)</li>
<li>Ltd. (Limited), Ltd. Co. (Limited Company): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">Limited partnerships</a>, companies with legal status use the <i>Inc.</i> and <i>Corp.</i> suffix unlike in other <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">SEA</a> countries.</li></ul>
<p>Older forms (now rarely used)
</p>
<ul><li>Cía (Compañía): for partnerships and other forms of business during the Spanish rule</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">SA</a> (Sociedad Anónima): formed under Spanish rule</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Poland">Poland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Poland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>jednoosobowa działalność gospodarcza: <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>Przedsiębiorstwo Państwowe: state enterprise (has <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legal_personality" title="Legal personality">legal personality</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (spółka akcyjna): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum share capital PLN 100,000 (approx. €25,000) (has <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legal_personality" title="Legal personality">legal personality</a>).</li>
<li>s.c. (spółka cywilna): "civil partnership", not a partnership or a company, but rather an agreement on the sharing of profits, losses and ownership of a business. Can be likened to a <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">voluntary association</a>.</li>
<li>S.K.A. (spółka komandytowo-akcyjna): limited partnership with shares. Minimum share capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zloty" title="Zloty">PLN</a> 50,000 (approx. €12,500).</li>
<li>sp.j. (spółka jawna): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>sp.k. (spółka komandytowa): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>sp.p. (spółka partnerska): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">limited liability partnership</a> May also be denoted by the addition of <i>i partner(zy)</i> ("and partner(s)") to the firm's name. Can only be used for the purpose of practicing as a licensed professional listed in the appropriate provision of the Commercial Companies Code. The partners are fully liable for the partnership's debts, with the exception of debts incurred by other partners practicing their licensed profession and employees under their direction.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_(polish)_limited_liability_company_(sp._z_o.o.)" title="The (polish) limited liability company (sp. z o.o.)">Sp. z o.o.</a> (spółka z ograniczoną odpowiedzialnością): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Minimum share capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zloty" title="Zloty">PLN</a> 5,000 (approx. €1,250) (has <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legal_personality" title="Legal personality">legal personality</a>).</li>
<li>Spółdzielnia: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a>. Has legal personality. May also be denoted by the word <i>Spółdzielczy</i> in the firm's name (has <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Legal_personality" title="Legal personality">legal personality</a>).</li></ul>
<p><small>References: (Polish) Commercial Companies Code of 15 September 2000 (Dz.U. N<sup>o</sup> 94 item 1037 as amended); (Polish) Civil Code of 23 April 1964 (Dz.U. N<sup>o</sup> 16 item 93 as amended); (Polish) Law on Cooperatives of 16 September 1982 (Dz.U. 2003 N<sup>o</sup> 188 item 1848 as amended)</small>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portugal">Portugal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Portugal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>CRL (Cooperativa de Responsabilidade Limitada): limited liability <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedade Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), and these are further classified as:
<ul><li>S.A., Sociedade Aberta: ≈ publicly traded corporation (literally "open company").</li>
<li>S.F., Sociedade Fechada: ≈ privately held (closely held) corporation (literally "closed company")</li></ul></li>
<li>Lda. (Limitada): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK), and these might be:
<ul><li>Unipessoal Lda.: single member company (literally: "Unipersonal Ltd.")</li></ul></li>
<li>SGPS (Sociedade Gestora de Participações Sociais): holding corporation (literally "shareholding management company")</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Romania">Romania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Romania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b><i>Societăți comerciale</i>, abbreviated SC (Companies):</b>
</p>
<ol><li><i><b>Societăți de persoane</b></i> <b>(Unincorporated companies, also called Partnerships)</b>
<ul><li><i>Societatea în nume colectiv</i>, abbreviated <i>SNC</i> (General Partnership, abbreviated GP)</li>
<li><i>Societatea în comandită simplă</i>, abbreviated <i>SCS</i> (Limited Partnership, abbreviated LP)</li></ul></li>
<li><i><b>Societăți de capitaluri</b></i> <b>(Incorporated companies, also called Corporations)</b>
<ul><li><i>Societatea în comandită pe acțiuni</i>, abbreviated <i>SCA</i> (Company Limited by Shares)</li>
<li><i>Societatea pe acțiuni</i>, abbreviated <i>SA</i> (Joint-Stock Company)</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Societăți hibride (Hybrid companies)</b>
<ul><li><i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Societate_cu_R%C4%83spundere_Limitat%C4%83" title="Societate cu Răspundere Limitată">Societate cu răspundere limitată</a></i>, abbreviated <i>SRL</i> (Limited Liability Company)</li>
<li><i>Societatea cu răspundere limitată cu proprietar unic</i>, abbreviated <i>SRL cu proprietar unic</i></li></ul></li></ol>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Societate pe Acţiuni): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>S.C.A. (societate în comandită pe acţiuni): limited partnership with shares</li>
<li>S.C.S. (societate în comandită simplă): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>S.N.C. (societate în nume colectiv): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>S.R.L. (societate cu răspundere limitată): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>PFA (persoana fizica autorizata): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-employed" title="Self-employed">self-employed</a> (UK) <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_Proprietorship" title="Sole Proprietorship">Sole Proprietorship</a> (US)</li>
<li>O.N.G. (Organizație Non-Guvernamentală): ≈ Non-state pension fund (literally: Non-Governmental Organization)</li></ol>
<p>limited liability company "societate cu raspundere limitata" (SRL);
joint stock company "societate pe actiuni" (SA);
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">Russia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Russia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Types_of_business_entity_in_Russia" title="Types of business entity in Russia">Types of business entity in Russia</a></div>
