Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">December 2018</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul><li>NKO/НКО, (Nekommercheskaya organizatsiya / Некоммерческая организация): non-profit organization. There are many types of non-profits in Russia; the type depends on the ownership of the assets <span class="clarify-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">(<a href="/wiki/Non-governmental_organization" title="Non-governmental organization">NGO</a> <a href="/wiki/Pension_Fund_of_the_Russian_Federation" title="Pension Fund of the Russian Federation">Pension Fund</a>, for instance)</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Clarify" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="how is this a good example? it introduces an NGO type of organization which is unclearly related to NKO (December 2018)">clarify</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>GP/ГП, GUP/ГУП (Gosudarstvennoye (unitarnoye) predpriyatiye / Государственное (унитарное) предприятие): state (unitary) enterprise</li>
<li>IP/ИП (Individualny predprinimatel' / Индивидуальный предприниматель): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>OOO/ООО (Obschestvo s ogranichennoy otvetstvennostyu / Общество с ограниченной ответственностью): <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a> (US)</li>
<li>PAO/ПАО (Publichnoye aktsionernoye obschestvo / Публичное акционерное общество): <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), publicly traded shares (similar to a corporation in the US)</li>
<li>Kooperativ/кооператив: cooperative (many types, which differ by the type of activity, e.g. agricultural or production)</li>
<li>АО/AO (Aktsionernoye obschestvo / Акционерное общество): <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">private limited company</a> (ltd) (UK), privately held shares (similar to a close corporation, or closely held corporation, in the US) (maximum fifty "owners of capital" (not shareholders); if there are more than fifty "owners of capital", they have a year to transform into a PAO)</li>
<li><a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%9F%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE" title="ru:Простое товарищество">Prostoye tovarishestvo / Простое товарищество</a> (general partnership) and <a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE_%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B5" title="ru:Товарищество на вере">Kommanditnoe tovarishestvo / Коммандитное товарищество</a> (limited partnership). These types of business entities are not popular (approximately 0.5% of the total number of business entities in Russia<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>).</li>
<li><a class="extiw" href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A5%D0%BE%D0%B7%D1%8F%D0%B9%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D0%BF%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%82%D0%BD%D1%91%D1%80%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE" title="ru:Хозяйственное партнёрство">Hozyaystvennoye partnyorstvo / Хозяйственное партнёрство</a> (business partnership).</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Saudi_Arabia">Saudi Arabia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Saudi Arabia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Private Limited Company ( شركة ذات مسئولية محدودة)</li>
<li>Joint-Stock company ( شركة مساهمة )</li>
<li>General Partnership Company ( شركة تضامن )</li>
<li>Limited Partnership (شركة التوصية البسيطة )</li>
<li>Foreign Company ( شركة أجنبية )</li>
<li>Individual Establishment ( مؤسسة فردية )</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbia">Serbia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Serbia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>d.o.o. / д.о.о. (<a href="/wiki/Dru%C5%A1tvo_sa_ograni%C4%8Denom_odgovorno%C5%A1%C4%87u" title="Društvo sa ograničenom odgovornošću">društvo sa ograničenom odgovornošću</a> / друштво са ограниченом одговорношћу): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Limited liability partnership</a> ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a>(UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Gesellschaft_mit_beschr%C3%A4nkter_Haftung" title="Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung">GmbH</a> (Germany).</li>
<li>d.d. д.д. or a.d. / a.д. (deoničarsko (<i>deoničko</i>) društvo / деоничарско (<i>деоничко</i>) друштво or akcionarsko društvo / aкционарско друштво) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Joint-stock_company" title="Joint-stock company">joint-stock company</a>, <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Germany)</li>
<li>preduzetnik (preduzetnik / предузетник): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a> (UK)</li>
<li>o.d. / о.д. (ortačko društvo / ортачко друштво): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a> (UK)</li>
<li>k.d. / к.д. (komanditno društvo / командитно друштво): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">Limited partnership</a> (UK)</li>
<li>j.p. / ј.п. (javno preduzeće / јавно предузеће): ≈ <a href="/wiki/State-owned_enterprise" title="State-owned enterprise">state-owned enterprise</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Singapore">Singapore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Singapore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Private Limited Company, Sole Proprietorship and Partnership are the predominant types of business found in Singapore.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[57]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>LLP (<a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">limited liability partnership</a>): owners have the flexibility of operating as a partnership while enjoying limited liability.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> An LLP can sue and be sued, acquire and hold property, and have a common seal.</li>
<li>Pte Ltd/Sdn Bhd (private limited company/Sendirian Berhad): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Maximum 50 shareholders. There also exist "exempt private companies", being either owned by no more than 20 non-corporate shareholders, or wholly state-owned and designated by the finance <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Political_minister" title="Political minister">minister</a> as exempt.</li>
<li>Ltd/Bhd (public limited company/Berhad): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). There also exist public companies limited by guarantee, which conduct non-profit activities; the finance minister may approve the registration of such companies without the addition of the word "Limited" or "Berhad" to the name.</li>
<li>Singapore subsidiary company is a popular term used for a form of Singapore business entity. A subsidiary company can have different structures but is essentially a Private Limited Company and so is a separate legal entity. Characteristics of a Singapore subsidiary company include: i) 100% foreign ownership is allowed, ii) the company enjoys low tax incentives as per a resident company, iii) repatriation of profits is allowed and iv) the minimum paid up capital required is S$1. v) As a legal person, a subsidiary company can sue and be sued by others.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>Other forms including Pte exist</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovakia">Slovakia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Slovakia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>a.s. (Akciová spoločnosť): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum share capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/EURO" title="EURO">EUR</a> €25,000. Must have a <a href="/wiki/Supervisory_board" title="Supervisory board">supervisory board</a> in addition to the management board.</li>
<li>s.r.o., spol. s r.o. (Spoločnosť s ručením obmedzeným): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>k.s. (Komanditná spoločnosť): ≈ LLP. or <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Limited liability partnership</a> (UK). Must have at least one "general partner" with unlimited liability.</li>
<li>v.o.s. (Verejná obchodná spoločnosť): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a> or unlimited partnership</li>
<li>družstvo: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">Cooperative</a></li>
<li>živnosť: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovenia">Slovenia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Slovenia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>d.d. (Delniška družba): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK)</li>
<li>d.o.o. (Družba z omejeno odgovornostjo): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK)</li>
<li>d.n.o. (Družba z neomejeno odgovornostjo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">Unlimited company</a> (UK)</li>
<li>k.d. (Komanditna družba): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">LP</a> (UK)</li>
<li>s.p. (Samostojni podjetnik): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a> (UK)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Africa">South Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: South Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Sole proprietorship/Alleeneienaar</li>
<li>Business trust/Trust</li>
<li>Partnership/Vennootskap</li>
<li>Companies/Maatskappye
<ul><li>Company limited by guarantee
<ul><li>Incorporated association not for gain/vereniging sonder winsoogmerk (section 21 company/artikel 21-maatskappy): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">nonprofit association</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Companies having a share capital
<ul><li>Private company/privaat maatskappy: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">private limited company</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">limited liability company</a> (US); has 1 or more <a href="/wiki/Shareholder" title="Shareholder">shareholders</a>, one or more directors. The name must end "(Pty) Ltd"; registration number ends /07. Registration number and directors' names must appear on all correspondence.
<ul><li>Section 53(b) company (unlimited liability company): ≈ professional limited liability company (PLLC) (US)</li></ul></li>
<li>Public company/publieke maatskappy (Ltd.): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">public limited company</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a> (US); has at least 7 shareholders (unless it is a wholly owned subsidiary of another company) and at least two <a href="/wiki/Board_of_directors" title="Board of directors">directors</a>. The company's name must end in "LTD"; its registration number ends in /06.</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>CC/BK (Close corporation/beslote korporasie): Has 1–10 non-corporate members. The name must end "CC" or "BK"; registration number ends /23. Registration number and members' names must appear on all correspondence. On 1 May 2011 the new Companies Act (Act 71 of 2008) came into force and disallows any new incorporations under this form.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[58]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Spain">Spain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Spain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedad Anónima): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), minimum capital €60,101.21</li>
<li>S.L. (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sociedad_de_responsabilidad_limitada" title="Sociedad de responsabilidad limitada">Sociedad Limitada</a>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK), minimum capital €3,012</li>
<li>S.L.N.E. (Sociedad Limitada Nueva Empresa): similar to S.L., it was introduced in 2003 to speed up new company registration (registration can be completed in one day), minimum capital €3,012</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sociedad_An%C3%B3nima_Deportiva" title="Sociedad Anónima Deportiva">S.A.D.</a> (Sociedad Anónima Deportiva): a limited liability sports corporation</li>
<li>S.L.L. (Sociedad Limitada Laboral): a labour limited corporation</li>
<li>S.C. (Sociedad Colectiva): roughly a <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>S.C.P. (Sociedad Civil Privada): ¿?</li>
<li>S.Cra. (Sociedad Comanditaria): roughly a <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>S.Coop. (Sociedad Cooperativa): a <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a> that typically is owned and democratically controlled by its workers
<ul><li>Other initialisations are used for cooperatives; Sociedad Anónima Laboral (SAL);<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[59]</a></sup> some are region specific e.g. Sociedad Cooperativa Catalana Limitada (SCCL)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[60]</a></sup></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sweden">Sweden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Sweden">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>AB (<a href="/wiki/Aktiebolag" title="Aktiebolag">Aktiebolag</a>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Minimum capital SEK 25,000.</li>
<li>AB (publ) (Publikt aktiebolag): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum capital <a href="/wiki/Swedish_krona" title="Swedish krona">SEK</a> 500,000.</li>
<li>Ek. för. (Ekonomisk förening): economic association (minimum three members)
<ul><li>Bostadsrättsförening: home-owners' association</li>
<li>Hyresrättsförening: home-renters' association</li>
<li>Kooperativ: <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Enskild firma: <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>HB (Handelsbolag): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>KB (Kommanditbolag): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>Enkelt bolag: Regulated partnership between two parts (Companies or private persons)</li>
<li>Ideell förening: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-profit_organization" title="Non-profit organization">non-profit organization</a></li>
<li>Stiftelse: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foundation_(nonprofit_organization)" title="Foundation (nonprofit organization)">Foundation</a> has capital or property but no members or owners (shareholders)</li>
<li>Filial</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Switzerland">Switzerland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Switzerland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Aktiengesellschaft" title="Aktiengesellschaft">AG</a> (Aktiengesellschaft)</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">SA</a> (Société anonyme)</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">SA</a> (Società anonima)</td>
<td>≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK) or <a href="/wiki/Incorporation_(business)" title="Incorporation (business)">Inc.</a> (US). Min. <a href="/wiki/Share_capital" title="Share capital">share capital</a> <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">CHF</a> 100,000. Bearer or registered shares, of a <a href="/wiki/Par_value" title="Par value">par value</a> of min. <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">CHF</a> 0.01 each. Details of shareholders generally not publicly available (except for main shareholders and management shares of publicly listed companies).
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GmbH" title="GmbH">GmbH</a> (Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung)</td>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A0rl" title="Sàrl">Sàrl</a> (Société à responsabilité limitée)</td>
<td>Sagl (Società a garanzia limitata)</td>
<td>≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US). Min. capital <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">CHF</a> 20,000. Registered shares only, of a <a href="/wiki/Par_value" title="Par value">par value</a> of min. <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">CHF</a> 100 each. Name, address and share of each owner (and any changes) publicly recorded in the Official Register of Commerce.&lt;<a class="external free" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110706221252/http://www.zefix.admin.ch/%3E" rel="nofollow">https://web.archive.org/web/20110706221252/http://www.zefix.admin.ch/%3E</a>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul><li>Stiftung / fondation / fondazione:≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foundation_(nonprofit_organization)" title="Foundation (nonprofit organization)">foundation</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Investment_fund" title="Investment fund">investment fund</a></i> (Anlagefonds / fonds de placement / fondo di investimento)
<ul><li>Investmentgesellschaft mit festem Kapital / SICAF (société d'investissement à capital fixe) / SICAF (società di investimento a capitale fisso):≈ <a href="/wiki/Investment_trust" title="Investment trust">investment trust</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Closed-end_fund" title="Closed-end fund">closed-end company</a> (US)</li>
<li>Investmentgesellschaft mit variablem Kapital / SICAV (société d'investissement à capital variable) / SICAV (società di investimento a capitale variabile):≈ OEIC (<a href="/wiki/Open-ended_investment_company" title="Open-ended investment company">open-ended investment company</a>) (UK), open-end company (US)</li></ul></li>
<li>Verein / association / associazione:≈ <a href="/wiki/Voluntary_association" title="Voluntary association">non-profit association</a></li>
<li>wIG (wirtschaftliche Interessengemeinschaft) / GIE (groupement d'intérêt économique) / gruppo di interesse economico:≈ EIG (economic interest grouping)</li>
<li><i lang="de" title="German language text">Einzelunternehmen / RI (raison individuelle) / ditta individuale</i>:≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_trader" title="Sole trader">sole trader</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a> (US)</li>
<li>Gesellschaft "business entities"
<ul><li><i>partnerships</i> (Rechsgemeinschaft / société de personnes / società di persone)
<ul><li>eG (einfache Gesellschaft) / société simple / società semplice:≈ partnership by contract</li>
<li>KolG (Kollektivgesellschaft) / SNC (société en nom collectif) / società in nome collettivo:≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">GP</a></li>
<li>KG (Kommanditgesellschaft) / SC (société en commandite) / società in accomandita:≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">LP</a></li></ul></li>
<li><i>trading companies</i> (Körperschaft / société de capitaux / società di capitale)
<ul><li>KomAG (Kommanditaktiengesellschaft) / SCA (société en commandite par actions) / società in accomandita per azioni:≈ publicly traded partnership (PTP)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GmbH" title="GmbH">GmbH</a> (Gesellschaft mit beschränkter Haftung) / <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A0rl" title="Sàrl">Sàrl</a> (société à responsabilité limitée) / Sagl (società a garanzia limitata):≈ <a href="/wiki/Private_limited_company" title="Private limited company">Ltd.</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a> (US)</li>
<li>AG (Aktiengesellschaft) / SA (société anonyme) / SA (società anonima):≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corp.</a> (US/Can)</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>Genossenschaft / Scoop (société coopérative) / società cooperativa:≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Co-operative" title="Co-operative">co-operative</a></li>
<li>Zweigniederlassung / succursale / succursale:≈ branch (of a company)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Taiwan">Taiwan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Taiwan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>無限公司 (Unlimited Company)</li>
<li>有限公司 (Limited Company, <i>yǒuxiàn gōngsī</i><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chinese.yabla.com_62-0"><a href="#cite_note-chinese.yabla.com-62">[61]</a></sup>)</li>
<li>兩合公司 (Limited Partnership)</li>
<li>股份有限公司 (Public Limited Company or Corporation, <i>gǔfèn yǒuxiàn gōngsī</i><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chinese.yabla.com_62-1"><a href="#cite_note-chinese.yabla.com-62">[61]</a></sup>)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Thailand">Thailand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Thailand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>บริษัทมหาชนจำกัด, name format บริษัท <i>corporation name</i> จำกัด (มหาชน): <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK). Minimum 15 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shareholders" title="Shareholders">shareholders</a>.</li>
<li>บริษัทเอกชนจำกัด (name format บริษัท <i>corporation name</i> จำกัด): <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). At least three shareholders.</li>
<li>ห้างหุ้นส่วนจำกัด (name format ห้างหุ้นส่วน <i>corporation name</i> จำกัด): <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a> There are two kinds of partnership: Limited partnership which has limited liability of the partnership, and unlimited partner which has unlimited liability to the third party for the partner. The unlimited partnership has the right to control the partnership. On the other hand, the limited partnership has no right to make decision in the partnership.</li>
<li>ห้างหุ้นส่วนสามัญนิติบุคคล (name format ห้างหุ้นส่วน <i>corporation name</i>): <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkey">Turkey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Turkey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>According to Code of Obligations (fifth book of Civil Code) (Act No: 6098):
</p>
<ul><li>Adi Şirket : ≈ <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Simple_Pprtnership&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Simple Pprtnership (page does not exist)">Simple Pprtnership</a> (has no legal personality)</li></ul>
<p>According to the Commercial Code (Act No: 6102):
</p><p>Şahıs şirketleri ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Partnerships" title="Partnerships">Partnerships</a> (Unlike the partnerships in Anglo-American law, they also have legal personality like companies)
</p>
<ul><li>Koll. Şti. (Kolektif şirket): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">Collective partnership</a></li>
<li>Kom. Şti (Komandit şirket) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Commandite partnership</a> Can be established as simple commandite partnership or as commandite company divided into shares (Sermayesi paylara bölünmüş komandit şirket).</li></ul>
<p>Sermaye şirketleri ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Companies" title="Companies">Companies</a>
</p>
<ul><li>A.Ş. / A.O. (<i lang="tr" title="Turkish language text">Anonim Şirket / Anonim Ortaklık</i>): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joint_stock_company" title="Joint stock company">Joint stock company</a> Minimum capital is <a href="/wiki/Turkish_lira" title="Turkish lira">TRY</a> 50,000. Bearer or registered shares, of a minimum <a href="/wiki/Par_value" title="Par value">par value</a> of TRY 0.01 each. Only type of company that can be publicly traded in Turkish Law.</li>
<li>Ltd. Şti. / L.Ş. / L.O. (Limited şirket / Limited Ortaklık) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_company" title="Limited company">Limited company</a> Minimum capital is TRY 10,000. Registered shares only, of a minimum <a href="/wiki/Par_value" title="Par value">par value</a> of TRY 25 each.</li></ul>
<p>According to the Capital Markets Act (Act No: 6362):
</p>
<ul><li>HAAO (<i lang="tr" title="Turkish language text">Halka Açık Anonim Ortaklık</i>) ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Publicly_held_corporation" title="Publicly held corporation">Publicly held corporation</a> This essentially is a special type of A.O. These type of companies can only be established as A.O.'s. When there are no specific rules under Capital Markets legislation, A.O. rules under Turkish Commercial Code will be applied to HAAO's.</li></ul>
<p>According to the Cooperatives Act (Act No: 1136):
</p>
<ul><li>Koop. (Kooperatif Şirket) ≈ <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">Cooperative</a></li></ul>
<p>Other entitites:
</p>
<ul><li>(irtibat bürosu): ≈ Liaison Office</li>
<li>Şahıs Firması: ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sole_Proprietorship" title="Sole Proprietorship">Sole Proprietorship</a></li>
<li>Şb. (Şube): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Branch" title="Branch">Branch</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tunisia">Tunisia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Tunisia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>شركة فردية (Entreprise individuelle)</li>
<li>شّركة ذات مسؤوليّات محدودة ش.م.م.(Société à responsabilité limitée- SARL)</li>
<li>شّركة فردية ذات مسؤوليّات محدودة (Société unipersonnelle à responsabilité limitée SUARL)</li>
<li>شركة خفية الإسم (Société anonyme – SA)</li>
<li>الشركات ذات رأس المال المتغيّر</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ukraine">Ukraine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Ukraine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Unreferenced_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg"><img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Referencing_for_beginners" title="Help:Referencing for beginners">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. <ul><li>DAT/ДАТ (Державне акціонерне товариство / Derzhavne aktsionerne tovarystvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), national</li>
<li>FOP/ФОП (Фізична особа підприємець / Fizychna osoba pidpryyemets): <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorship</a></li>
<li>KT/КТ (Командитне товариство / Komandytne tovarystvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">limited partnership</a></li>
<li>PT/ПT (Повне товариство / Povne tovarystvo): ≈ <a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">general partnership</a></li>
<li>TDV/ТДВ (Товариство з додатковою відповідальністю / Tovarystvo z dodatkvoiu vidpovidalnistiu): "additional liability company"</li>
<li>TOV/TOB (Товариство з обмеженою відповідальністю / Tovarystvo z obmezhenoiu vidpovidalnistiu): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). Minimum capital = 1 minimum wage (UAH 960 as of 29.05.2011<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>).</li>
<li>PP/ПП (Приватне підприємство / Pryvatne pidpryyemstvo): ≈ <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ltd." title="Ltd.">Ltd.</a> (UK). No minimum capital.</li>
<li>VAT/ВАТ( Вiдкрите акцiонерне товариство / Vidkryte aktsionerne tovarystvo) or PAT/ПАТ (Публічне акціонерне товариство / Publichne aktsionerne tovarystvo) since 29.04.2009: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), public. Minimum capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hryvnia" title="Hryvnia">UAH</a> 630,000.</li>
<li>ZAT/ЗАТ (Закрите акцiонерне товариство / Zakryte Aktsionerne Tovarystvo)or PrAT/ПрАТ (Приватне акціонерне товариство / Prytvatne aktsionerne tovarystvo) since 29.04.2009: ≈ <a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company">plc</a> (UK), private.</li>
<li>AT/АТ (Акціонерне товариство / Aktsionerne tovarystvo): ≈ JSC.</li></ul>
<p>Company formation is regulated by the Ukrainian Civil Code and Commercial Code, Law of Commercial companies, Law of stock companies, law and order.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>CIC (<a href="/wiki/Community_interest_company" title="Community interest company">community interest company</a>)</li>
<li>CIO (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charitable_Incorporated_Organisation" title="Charitable Incorporated Organisation">Charitable Incorporated Organisation</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Industrial_and_provident_society" title="Industrial and provident society">Industrial and provident society</a>: e.g. a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Co-operative" title="Co-operative">co-operative</a> (which does include Ltd. at the end of its name) or charity</li>
<li><b>Partnerships</b>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LLP" title="LLP">LLP</a> (<a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">Limited liability partnership</a>)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scottish_limited_partnerships" title="Scottish limited partnerships">Scottish limited partnerships</a></li>
<li>LP (<a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">Limited partnership</a>)</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Companies</b><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Companies_Act_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-Companies_Act-63">[62]</a></sup>
<ul><li><b>Private Limited Companies</b> (<i>Ltd</i> or <i>Limited</i> or  Welsh <i>Cyfyngedig</i> (<i>Cyf</i>))
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_shares" title="Private company limited by shares">Private company limited by shares</a></b>, The liability is limited to the amount, if any, unpaid on the shares held by them. Its shares cannot be traded publicly.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Private_company_limited_by_guarantee" title="Private company limited by guarantee">Private company limited by guarantee</a></b>. The liability is limited to such amount as the members undertake to contribute to the assets of the company in the event of its being wound up.</li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Public_limited_company" title="Public limited company"><b>Public Limited Company</b></a> (<i>PLC</i> or Welsh <i>Cwmni Cyfyngedig Cyhoeddus</i> (<i>CCC)</i>): Is a limited company whose <a href="/wiki/Share_(finance)" title="Share (finance)">shares</a> may be traded publicly. Requires an authorized minimum <a href="/wiki/Share_capital" title="Share capital">share capital</a> of £50,000;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-business-link-set-up_64-0"><a href="#cite_note-business-link-set-up-64">[63]</a></sup> of which it must have allotted shares to the value of at least £50,000 and a minimum of 25% must be fully paid up prior to starting business.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Unlimited_company" title="Unlimited company">Unlimited company</a></b> (or Welsh (<i>cwmni</i>) <i>anghyfyngedig</i>). There is no limit on the liability of its members. It is not a requirement under company law to add or state the word or designation Unlimited or its abbreviations (Unltd., or Ultd.) at the ending of its legal company name, and most such companies do not do so. Unlimited companies are exempted from filing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Financial_statements" title="Financial statements">accounts</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Registrar_of_Companies" title="Registrar of Companies">Registrar of Companies</a> for public disclosure, subject to a few exceptions (unless the company was a qualified subsidiary or a parent of a limited company during the accounting period).</li></ul></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a></b> (Sole traders)</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">United States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: United States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the United States, most businesses are incorporated under the law of a particular state. The federal government does not generally incorporate entities, with a few narrow exceptions.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tax_classifications">Tax classifications</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Tax classifications">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>For federal tax purposes, the <a href="/wiki/Internal_Revenue_Service" title="Internal Revenue Service">Internal Revenue Service</a> has separate <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Entity_classification" title="Entity classification">entity classification</a> rules. Under the tax rules, an entity may be classified as a <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Partnership" title="Partnership">partnership</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">cooperative</a> or a disregarded entity. A corporation may be taxed as either a <a href="/wiki/C_corporation" title="C corporation">C corporation</a> or elect to be treated as a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Subchapter_S_corporation" title="Subchapter S corporation">Subchapter S corporation</a>. A disregarded entity has one owner (or a married couple as owner) that is not recognized for tax purposes as an entity separate from its owner. Types of disregarded entities include single-member <a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLCs</a>; qualified sub-chapter S subsidiaries and qualified <a href="/wiki/Real_estate_investment_trust" title="Real estate investment trust">real estate investment trust</a> subsidiaries. A disregarded entity's transparent tax status does not affect its status under state law. For example, for federal tax purposes, a sole-member LLC (SMLLC) is disregarded, so that all its assets and liabilities are treated as owned by its single member. But under state law, an SMLLC can contract in its own name and its owner is generally not personally liable for the debts and obligations of the entity.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Presti_and_Naegele_Newsletter_65-0"><a href="#cite_note-Presti_and_Naegele_Newsletter-65">[64]</a></sup> To be recognized as a <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">Cooperative</a> for tax purposes Cooperatives must follow certain rules under Sub Chapter T of the <a href="/wiki/Internal_Revenue_Code" title="Internal Revenue Code">Internal Revenue Code</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IRS_Sub_Chapter_T_66-0"><a href="#cite_note-IRS_Sub_Chapter_T-66">[65]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Federally_incorporated">Federally incorporated</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Federally incorporated">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Of the few types of companies that may exist under a federally issued charter, the bulk are <a href="/wiki/Bank" title="Bank">banks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Credit_union" title="Credit union">credit unions</a>, and similar <a href="/wiki/Depository_institution" title="Depository institution">depository institutions</a>. Such institutions are distinguished from state-chartered banks by including a key word in their formal names. For a bank, the key word is "national". A bank chartered by the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_the_Comptroller_of_the_Currency" title="Office of the Comptroller of the Currency">Office of the Comptroller of the Currency</a> (OCC) must have the word "national" in its name. A bank chartered by a state cannot have "national" in its name.
</p><p>For a savings bank (formerly called a savings and loan association) or credit union, the key word is "federal", and the same rules apply; a federally chartered savings bank or credit union must have the word "federal" in its name, while a state chartered savings bank or credit union cannot have "federal" in its name.
</p>
<ul><li>FSB (<a href="/wiki/Federal_savings_bank" title="Federal savings bank">Federal Savings Bank</a>), formerly called federal savings and loan association</li>
<li>NA (<a href="/wiki/National_bank#United_States" title="National bank">National Association</a>), a designation used by banks chartered by the Office of the Comptroller of the Currency (OCC)</li>
<li>NT&amp;SA (<a href="/wiki/National_Trust_and_Savings_Association" title="National Trust and Savings Association">National Trust and Savings Association</a>), a less common designation used by national banks</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Credit_union#United_States" title="Credit union">Federal Credit Union</a>, chartered by the National Credit Union Association (NCUA)</li></ul>
<p>Many federal governmental units are specially formed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government-owned_corporation" title="Government-owned corporation">public corporations</a>, while some private organizations have received a <a href="/wiki/Congressional_charter" title="Congressional charter">charter from Congress</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="State.2C_territory_or_commonwealth_incorporated"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="State,_territory_or_commonwealth_incorporated">State, territory or commonwealth incorporated</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: State, territory or commonwealth incorporated">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/United_States_corporate_law" title="United States corporate law">United States corporate law</a>, <a href="/wiki/Delaware_General_Corporation_Law" title="Delaware General Corporation Law">Delaware General Corporation Law</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nevada_corporation" title="Nevada corporation">Nevada corporation</a></div>
<p>The following are the main business designations and types:
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">Sole proprietorship</a></b>: a business consisting of a single owner (which may in turn be a business entity), not in a separately recognized business form.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Trust_company" title="Trust company">Trust</a></b></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Partnerships">Partnerships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Partnerships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/General_partnership" title="General partnership">General partnership</a></b>: a partnership in which all the partners are jointly and separately liable for the debts of the partnership. In most U.S. states, it can be created by agreement without requiring a public filing. The partners may themselves be legal entities or individuals.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Limited_partnership" title="Limited partnership">LP</a> (<b>Limited partnership)</b>: a partnership where at least one partner (the general partner, which may itself be an entity or an individual) has unlimited liability for the LP's debts and one or more partners (the limited partners) have limited liability (which means that they are not responsible for the LP's debts beyond the amount they agreed to invest). Limited partners generally do not participate in the management of the entity or its business.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_partnership" title="Limited liability partnership">LLP</a> (<b>Limited Liability Partnership)</b>: a partnership where a partner's liability for the debts of the partnership is limited except in the case of liability for acts of professional negligence or malpractice. In some states, LLPs may only be formed for purposes of practicing a licensed profession, typically attorneys, accountants and architects. This is often the only form of limited partnership allowed for law firms (as opposed to general partnerships).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_limited_partnership" title="Limited liability limited partnership">LLLP</a> (<b>Limited Liability Limited Partnership)</b>: a combination of LP and LLP, available in some states.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Limited_Liability_Companies">Limited Liability Companies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Limited Liability Companies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company" title="Limited liability company">LLC</a>, LC, Ltd. Co., (<b>Limited Liability Company)</b>: a form of business whose owners enjoy limited liability, but which is not a <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporation</a>. Allowable abbreviations vary by state. Note that in some states <i>Ltd.</i> by itself is not a valid abbreviation for an LLC, because in some states (e.g. <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>), it may denote a corporation instead. See also <a href="/wiki/Series_LLC" title="Series LLC">Series LLC</a>. For U.S. federal tax purposes, in general, an LLC with two or more members is treated as a partnership, and an LLC with one member is treated as a sole proprietorship.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Limited_liability_company#Variations" title="Limited liability company">PLLC</a> (<b>Professional Limited Liability Company)</b>: some states do not allow certain professionals to form an LLC that would limit the liability that results from the services professionals provide such as doctors, medical care; lawyers, legal advice; and accountants, accounting services; architects, architectural services; when the company formed offers the services of the professionals. Instead those states allow a PLLC or in the LLC statutes, the liability limitation only applies to the business side, such as creditors of the company, as opposed to the client/customer service side, the level of medical care, legal services, or accounting provided to clients. This is meant to maintain the higher ethical standards that these professionals have committed themselves to by becoming licensed in their profession and to prevent them from being immune (or at least limit their immunity) to malpractice suits.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Corporations">Corporations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Corporations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">Corp.</a>, (<b>Corporation), <a href="/wiki/Incorporation_(business)" title="Incorporation (business)">Inc.</a>, (Incorporated)</b>: used to denote <a href="/wiki/Corporation" title="Corporation">corporations</a> (<a href="/wiki/Public_company" title="Public company">public</a> or otherwise). These are the only terms universally accepted by all 51 corporation chartering jurisdictions in the United States. However, in some states other suffixes may be used to identify a corporation, such as Ltd., Co./Company, or the Italian term S.p.A. (in <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">Connecticut</a>; see under <a href="#Italy">Italy</a>). Some states that allow the use of "Company" prohibit the use of "and Company", "and Co.", "&amp; Company" or "&amp; Co.". In most states <a href="/wiki/Sole_proprietorship" title="Sole proprietorship">sole proprietorships</a> and partnerships may register a fictitious "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doing_business_as" title="Doing business as">doing business as</a>" name with the word "Company" in it. For a full list of allowed designations by state, see the table below.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Professional_corporation" title="Professional corporation">Professional corporation</a></b>, (PC or P.C.): those corporate entities for which many corporation statutes make special provision, regulating the use of the corporate form by licensed professionals such as attorneys, architects, accountants, and doctors.</li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doing_Business_As" title="Doing Business As">Doing Business As</a></b>: denotes a business name used by a person or entity that is different from the person's or entity's true name. DBAs are not separate entities and do not shield the person or entity who uses the DBA as a business name from liability for debts or lawsuits. Filing requirements vary and are not permitted for some types of businesses or professional practices.  See also <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delaware_corporation" title="Delaware corporation">Delaware corporation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Delaware_statutory_trust" title="Delaware statutory trust">Delaware statutory trust</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nevada_corporation" title="Nevada corporation">Nevada corporation</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_business_trust" title="Massachusetts business trust">Massachusetts business trust</a>.</li></ul>
<p>Required designations for corporations, by U.S. state, territory or commonwealth:

<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a></td>
<td>"corporation", "incorporated", "company", or "limited", or the abbreviation "corp.", "inc.", "co.", or "ltd."</td>
<td>§ 13.1-630. Code of Virginia
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_(U.S._state)" title="Washington (U.S. state)">Washington</a></td>
<td>"corporation", "incorporated", "company", or "limited", or the abbreviation "corp.", "inc.", "co.", or "ltd."; must not include "Bank", "banking", "banker", "trust", "cooperative", or any combination of the words "industrial" and "loan", or any combination of any two or more of the words "building", "savings", "loan", "home", "association", and "society"</td>
<td>§ 23B.04.010 Revised Code of Washington
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">West Virginia</a></td>
<td>"corporation", "incorporated", "company" or "limited", or the abbreviation "corp.", "inc.", "co." or "ltd.", or words or abbreviations of like import in another language</td>
<td>§ 31D-4-401 West Virginia Code
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a></td>
<td>"corporation", "incorporated", "company" or "limited" or the abbreviation "corp.", "inc.", "co." or "ltd." or words or abbreviations of like import in another language</td>
<td>§ 180.0401 Wisconsin Statutes (for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stock_corporation" title="Stock corporation">Stock corporations</a>) and § 181.0401 Wisconsin Statutes (for <a href="/wiki/Non-stock_corporation" title="Non-stock corporation">non-stock corporations</a>)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Wyoming" title="Wyoming">Wyoming</a></td>
<td>Unclear; apparently any of "corporation", "company", "incorporated", and probably the usual abbreviations of "Corp." "Co." and "Inc."</td>
<td>§ 17-16-401 Wyoming Statutes
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uruguay">Uruguay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=93" title="Edit section: Uruguay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/S.A._(corporation)" title="S.A. (corporation)">S.A.</a> (Sociedad Anónima). Company by shares.</li>
<li>S.A.S. (Sociedad por Acciones Simplificada). A simplified version of the S.A.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Private_Limited_company" title="Private Limited company">S.R.L.</a> (Sociedad de Responsabilidad Limitada). Limited liability company.</li>
<li>S.C.I. (Sociedad de Capital e Industria). A company with segregated shares between capital and labor.</li>
<li>S.C. (Sociedad Colectiva). A company with unlimited liability between its members.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=94" title="Edit section: Uzbekistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>MChJ (Mas'uliyati Cheklangan Jamiyat/Масъулияти Чекланган Жамият): limited liability company</li>
<li>QMJ (Qo'shimcha ma'suliyatli jamiyat/Қўшимча масъулиятли жамият): additional liability company</li>
<li>AJ (Aksiyadorlik jamiyati/Акциядорлик жамияти): joint-stock company
<ul><li>OAJ (Ochiq aksiyadorlik jamiyati/Очиқ акциядорлик жамияти): public joint-stock company</li>
<li>YoAJ (Yopiq aksiyadorlik jamiyati/Ёпиқ акциядорлик жамияти): closed joint-stock company</li></ul></li>
<li>XK (Xususiy korxona/Хусусий корхона): private company</li>
<li>XT (Xususiy tadbirkorlik/Хусусий тадбиркорлик): sole proprietorship</li>
<li>OK (Oilaviy korxona/Оилавий корхона): family company</li>
<li>UK (Unitar korxona/Унитар корхона): unitary enterprise</li>
<li>QK (Qo'shma korxona/Қўшма корхона): joint venture</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Vietnam">Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_legal_entity_types_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=95" title="Edit section: Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Cty TNHH (Công ty trách nhiệm hữu hạn / "Company with Limited Liablity"): Limited Liability Company</li>
<li>Cty TNHH MTV (Công ty trách nhiệm hữu hạn một thành viên/ "Limited Liablity Company with a Single member") since 2005</li>
<li>Cty CP (Công ty cổ phần / "Company with Joint Stock"): Joint Stock Company</li>
<li>Công ty hợp danh / "Company of Partners": Partnership</li>
<li>Doanh nghiệp hợp danh / "Enterprise Partnership": Partnership</li>
<li>DNNN (Doanh nghiệp nhà nước / "Enterprise of the State"): State-Owned Enterprise</li>
<li>DNTN (Doanh nghiệp tư nhân / "Enterprise Private"): Proprietorship</li>
<li>DTNN (Doanh nghiệp có vốn đầu tư nước ngoài "Enterprise with Foreign Investment"): Foreign Investment Enterprise</li>
<li>HTX (Hợp tác xã/ Co-operation)</li>
<li>Chi nhánh : Branch Company</li>
<li>Nhóm Cty (Công Ty / "Group Company"): Holding Company</li></ul>
